Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee  

Foreword  
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)  
Go with the Resolve to Die  
<Summary of the Words> In 1960, I promised to embark on a three-year journey, and already two years have passed, leaving only one year remaining. I constantly think about how to spend this year. Move with the determination to dedicate yourself fully to achieve victorious results for the purpose.  
Where do you stand?  
This purpose is not only the Master's purpose, nor is it only the purpose of the current members. It is the will of the Master, the unified members, this land, the heavens, and God the Father. This is a grand and astonishing purpose. We have come through many paths of persecution and various circumstances over the past two years.  
When we consider the value of our self today and think about the issues of today and tomorrow, it may be said that we have fought well for this purpose. Of course, it may have also provoked others.  
When we think of the past where heaven cooperated, we must ask ourselves if we have become someone who can be worshipped by heaven and earth. This is a time to reflect. This purpose is not concluded; if we fall in front, we must step over and achieve it. Even if we fall,  
please fulfill this purpose in my stead. Thus, I reflect on my history.  
July 1, 1962 (Sunday) Evening Service, Former Headquarters Church.  
* This message was compiled from notes taken by Chairman Yoo Kwang-ryeol of the History Compilation Committee. The title was added by the editor.  
8 Go with the Resolve to Die  
Even if it means leaving a will that can be inherited, one must fall.  
The present is more important than the past, and the future is more important than the present. We must stand on the reality and march towards the world of purpose. If we make a mistake, it is not the past cooperation that becomes an issue, but rather a natural lamentation. Not only my life but also my ancestors and descendants are all involved. If the past is holy, the steps we take will also be noble.  
When asked whether you are a victor or a loser, where do you stand now? We must once again reassess ourselves.  
Can you come and go freely through the church doors? You cannot. The name of the Father called here is not a name that can be called so easily, nor is the noun "family" that we call here something that can be called easily. It is built upon the foundation of countless saints' blood and sweat.  
The mere fact of coming to this holy place is not the issue. In other words, it is not the act of listening to a sermon that is the issue, but rather my own self that is the problem. We must critically examine whether there is a tendency for conventional faith concepts or habitual living to continue.  
Since you were born anyway, you must live and eventually leave. Being born is not something that is declared from the beginning, nor is living something that is declared as living.  
If a person is born with something of value, they must live such a life and then go to the next world. They must live such a life.  
Since I came from a solemn place, I must live in a solemn place and go to a solemn place. This is not something that is done by someone else's command. It must start from natural connections and go towards the path of natural connections. However, it seems that one is born unnaturally, lives in an unnatural place, and goes to an unnatural place.  
Is it acceptable to live like this? No, it is not.  
Since one was born unnaturally, this must be resolved, and since one is living unnaturally, this must also be resolved, and since one is going unnaturally, this too must be resolved. However, this cannot be resolved by oneself. When one tries to resolve this and seek re-approval, God wants to intervene in your life, that is, in your life and death.  
9  
Our ancestors have placed a shameful responsibility on God for 6,000 years. Because God has not been able to shed that responsibility until now, humanity is in an unwanted position today. How great must have been the sorrow of the ancestors looking at this result? On the other hand, how great were the demands of heaven, and how great was heaven's labor?  
If one of you does well, the heavens and earth do well, and if one of you does poorly, the heavens and earth do poorly because of the historical connections behind it. There is a matter of raising a victorious banner and inheriting it to future generations along with your name.  
What is the purpose of your joining the church? What does it mean to be called a family in our church? Since we have not resolved what must be resolved on a familial, national, and heavenly level, we must resolve it individually before it can be resolved as a family. It is not for anyone's blessing.  
Do not stand in a position of betrayal.  
I was not born in a condition where I could be born in heaven with a connection of love, nor was I born in a condition where there is no enemy of love. To resolve this, one must first completely settle personal issues before the issues of heaven and earth can be resolved. One must leave no conditions for the future. One must resolve the sorrowful connections behind it. When examining oneself, one must resolve the issue of oneself, which is in tatters. That is my past, present, and future. What I boast of is my own self, my current position today.  
The past is shameful, and the present is shameful. How will I resolve all this shame before heaven and earth in my lifetime? I must resolve the past and the present, and I must resolve it under the recognition of heaven and earth, and I must once again resolve to have such a self for at least one hour in my lifetime from this moment.  
In my life for the purpose, I must hold onto something that cannot be changed even if I give everything from the past.  
Is there anyone who can claim that Abel, Noah, Abraham, or Moses had such an hour? No, there is not. That is why they cannot raise their faces in the spirit world.  
10 Go with the Resolve to Die  
The purpose of the Savior's second coming is to introduce a path that heaven can recognize after it has been resolved. Without doing this, there is no relationship between us and the messianic thought. With that, we cannot claim to be victors over Satan. This cannot be denied.  
We must have such a day. We must have a day that can be admired by heaven and earth, a day that can be said to have lived in accordance with the will of providence.  
Before such solemn tasks and matters that need repentance, having come here today, we must face both my past self and my current self. The past establishes the present. In other words, the present becomes the foundation for the future. This moment is a solemn point in time that determines whether we will pave the way for tomorrow or not.  
Therefore, there can be no carelessness on the path towards the purpose. There is no one to relax with. Recently, we must once again step up our efforts. If you wish to be praised, it is God's position to push you into such a place. God continuously emphasizes that we must rise above the reality of life and move towards a new future. Even in your irresponsibility, God has taken responsibility and has worked. The more you feel this, the more you should feel guilty for eating and being full, and you should feel guilty for being healthy.  
Even if your body is sick, you must feel that it is a shame to waste even an hour. There is a heaven that tells you to go for even one more hour, even in the face of death.  
I have met many people during this time. Those who swore with tears and snot, those who thought they would go even if the world could not, have all gone somewhere. Regardless of that tears and that oath, they have all gone to their own places. Those who have left may be at peace, but they have brought shame to the bond they swore with heaven.  
Pray to God about what kind of damage has been caused because of me. God wanted to establish the dignity and face of heaven by raising me, so it is absurd to pray. Jesus came as the prince of heaven but was labeled a traitor of the nation and disappeared in the dew of the cross, saying, "Not my will, but your will be done." He sought to establish the dignity and face of heaven until the moment of his death. Even in the Garden of Gethsemane, bleeding and dying, he cried out, "Not my will, but your will be done." You must not stand in a position of betrayal to heaven, even in the face of death.  
The path we walk begins with death, so we must place death before us and walk with the resolve to die. Let us go! Everyone is equally tired and faces difficulties. Let us go! We have different ideological standards. Let us go even to the place where harsh winds blow and the waves of death flow. Let us go even to the place where the weather is bad and the wind is blowing. Compare the past when we climbed Baegun Mountain with now. In the past, there were four people who climbed Baegun Mountain while carrying babies. How many are there now?  
Devote Yourself Fully for the Three-Year Period  
Until now, the path of the Unification Church has faced many external persecutions. For 40 years, I have not been able to live a single day with peace of mind. There has been great persecution from the spirit world and from the outside, both inside and out. That is why the teacher said,  
"How long until I cross the 40 hills? Time, hurry up and pass." It was incredibly difficult to cross the 40 hills.  
Connecting it with the poor, I have walked for 40 years, which was the path of restoration. Now it is being shortened. It is the path of indemnity and restoration. The three-year period must be devoted fully. It is a path of life and death that must be fought for, involving individuals, families, and nations.  
Having held events during this three-year period, I felt a bit relieved. I have endured so much hardship to come this far; in the beginning, there was much persecution starting from the spirit world. If it is done through the Word, Satan cannot set conditions. When heaven commands, we must receive a counterattack before Satan.  
Persecution arises not only from oneself but also from the triangular reactions between the spirit world and the earthly realm. In the past, I could not even go to a theater, and I could not show my calves or arms; I lived in hiding, even washing my face in places where I could not be seen. I lived separated from the world of Satan. Now, even if it is not clear whether I am living a life of faith outwardly, I have come to a place where Satan cannot accuse me.  
12 Go with the Resolve to Die  
Even during last year's blessing ceremony, the counterattacks were severe. After gaining a victorious foundation, it will be fine. Since heaven has done this, you must also do the same. What you leave behind during these three years should be, since this is my period, a contribution, even if small. By passing through this period, you must establish yourselves, recognized by heaven, based on the past, and establish the present based on the present. The future people must also walk.  
Until this year, you will face internal persecution. Once you get past this, it will be hard to enter. It will be so noisy to enter. Therefore, I will leave for a tour the day after tomorrow (July 4). That day is a significant day.  
This public tour during the three-year period may be the last. For this time, have the heart to tour together. When representing the whole, be especially mindful.  
If you devote yourselves fully during such a period, you will live. I will be gone for eight days, so I hope you will unite with the president and pray together.  
2)  
Become a Victor with Unchanging Belief  
<Summary of the Words> This place, Beomeo-dong in Busan, is a place that has faced indescribable persecution while starting the path of purpose, so it can be a place of sorrow. However, today, I will shake off such feelings and speak.  
Patience, Belief, and Responsibility  
When walking such a path, knowing that God first grieves before the teacher does, we must resolve to face all difficulties to comfort God's heart. Just as the loyal subjects of the past went forth, risking their parents' opposition and shedding noble blood, we must sow blood, sweat, and tears on this earth with God's heart.  
We must establish a connection with God and set a tradition as we are to create a new world of culture.  
The teacher hopes that those local members who are fighting for this purpose today will not fall.  
We must become a group that takes responsibility when the nation is in difficulty, and we must also be a group that takes responsibility for the difficulties of the present age. The world is relative. Even the United States, which boasts of being the top advanced cultural country, may find itself in the lowest position, and our nation, which is in the lowest position, can become the greatest nation. Therefore, we must be the ones who can take responsibility when this nation is in difficulty.  
If there are those who endure the difficulties of the present with hope for the future and steadfastly move forward, even if their appearance is shabby, God will raise such individuals.  
We must be aware that we are to inherit God's great work and must always be alert. Although we are in a humble position now, we must have the belief that one day we will stand in the highest position. A nation that carries this belief to the end will become the creators of a new culture.  
In one's lifetime, one must become someone who does not abandon their resolution, no matter what difficulties arise. You must think about what path you must take and what you must do. You must also understand the value of what you want to do.  
You must become someone who can embrace the universe. You must have the belief that you can move forward without falling, even when a typhoon comes. With this belief, you must become someone who can withstand issues of a national, religious, and ideological nature.  
In the future, there will be religious confusion and spiritual turmoil. People are unaware of this. The path of virtue is to know what will come at the end of life and to ignore the current pain. Those of you who have stepped into the Unification Church must be able to step forth, leaving behind everything you have lived until now.  
We must fight against the world. Until now, many prophets have fallen on the first trial path of external conditions. However, we must overcome this and go to the second trial path.  
Today, in terms of politics, economy, and culture, we cannot keep up with the world. Those who walk the path of virtue may appear to be in a poor state outwardly, but outwardly...
is a belief that can call for a meeting at the end with those who boast about their status. Who would have thought that such groups have been the backbone of today's global ideologies? When these groups do not fall but continue to advance and triumph, they become revered by all.

Religion supports the connection between God, myself, and the world. Practitioners have endured hardships not just for a day or two but throughout their lives, solely looking to God. Therefore, it cannot be said that they do not know God. Practitioners do not lament the path of suffering even at the time of their death. Rather, they wish for their descendants to walk the same path.

The Mission of Religion
What is truth? It is the same from beginning to end. Truth and principles do not change eternally, even as everything else transforms. A practitioner is someone who does not tolerate Satan, the enemy of the cosmos, and looks forward to the unchanging world.

Then, what should a practitioner do? A practitioner should not aim to establish the sovereignty of a nation but should take the ultimate purpose of avenging the enemy of heaven.

The one who comes to strike the world of evil is the Messiah, the Savior. This person has an ideology that can assert itself regarding the world after the end times. This ideology encompasses all virtues of this world, such as loyalty, filial piety, and zeal. From this perspective, Christianity must resolve all historical tragedies and fulfill the world of hope that God has desired for 6,000 years, returning the glory of victory to God. Thus, it must be said that God is true. Forever and ever, glory shall be.

Then, who is the opponent you must fight? It is not the enemy of a limited nation or a family but the enemy of heaven, that is, Satan.

We must endure until all painful things pass. To endure, we must equip ourselves internally and externally. Thus, we must become a beacon that clearly illuminates the world ahead.

As long as the heartbeat does not cease, we must long for the foundation of the new world, the desired garden, and the new self. Where should we begin to confront this? It must start from the small family.

Become victors with unchanging belief
Only then will we shine before heaven.

Those gathered here must unite as one to silently step forward to eliminate the enemy of heaven, the great enemy. When united and then dispersed, you must be the ones who can shake the Gyeongnam region.

When the teacher first set out on the path in Busan, he looked the same as others, but internally there was a significant difference. With the heart to resolve God's historical grievances concerning towns and villages, we must confront and overcome any difficulties that arise. We are in a position to be responsible for heaven and earth, the past, present, and future, so we must move vigorously.

This three-year period of evangelism has been established with God's will. You, who are present here, may seem insignificant externally and may be ridiculed by many, but you are being positioned to bow your heads in front of the nation and the world in the future. This is the teacher's plan. The teacher has lived for 40 years looking forward to this. However, since that day has not yet arrived, we must carry on with our beliefs until that day comes.

We are those who do good works for a good purpose. Therefore, you must endure, biting your lips, until the day you can stand in a good position with God and command. The teacher has also done so until now. For that, we must first give glory to God. Until then, let us endure and endure again. Let us bear hardships and injustices until the time comes.

We are a group that must find and establish not only this nation but also the world. Since you are in such a position, you must not yield no matter where you are sent. The question is who remains until the end at the brink of death. The one who remains until the end is the precious one.

You must have the disposition to encompass several nations. If you are assigned to a region, you will stand in the position of a sentinel in that area. Therefore, you must understand that if you fall, the whole will fall.

You must become someone who can shake things up in your assigned area. You must be able to convey from the lowest position to the highest position. With this belief, you should be able to fight for at least three years, or ten years.

Those who have done great things in history were not intellectuals. It was determined by who loved the nation and the people more. Even if your outward appearance is insignificant, you must have a heart that is loyal to the cause.

Be a lamp that brightens the world
The term unification means to gather and become one. To create oneness, we must break, carve, and refine what already exists. Who is this for? It is not for me but to please God. Regardless of who it is, going through this formal process is the principle. Going through this is not for me but for heaven.

In whatever we do, belief is the issue. Therefore, even if you suffer in your assigned area, you must live and act with faith. When we watch movies, we enjoy thrilling scenes. Similarly, when we work, we must overcome such thrilling moments well, as heaven, earth, and all creation hope for our victory.

When catching fish with a net, we must move forward even a little more to catch even one more fish. We are in a position like this net, so we must move with the desire to lead even one more person from the realm of Satan to God's side.

As we seek the path of virtue, we must resolve historical grievances. When we are negligent, God will be saddened, and when we make mistakes, God will be heartbroken. Therefore, we must become those who will break down the enemy's barriers with all our strength and sincerity and subdue Satan to resolve God's grievances. To do this, we must unite emotionally and move resolutely. When we move like this, we can cross into enemy territory. I hope you become those who move under this belief.

You are like a lit candle. In this stormy time, you must become candles that light the way. If we cannot become one, then two; if two cannot work, then three; even more than that, we must light up the world of darkness. Satan seeks to extinguish this candlelight. It does not just want to extinguish the flame but to destroy the candle itself. You must not become a collapsing candle.

The teacher aims to overthrow the world of Satan's grievances. And it must be done. You, who follow the teacher, must not become debtors before the master. You must become a group that the teacher can confidently send out to the pioneering areas. You must become a group that can establish the Gyeongnam region before the will and, further, establish the five oceans and six continents before the will.

You have walked hundreds of miles to attend here. The downfall of this nation was not due to a lack of money. Even if you appear in tattered clothing and with nothing, you must become someone who can be called the best in belief. We must become those with substance. Let us be those who are externally poor but infinitely rich internally.

We must know that we are not a group that exists alone; if we do not fulfill the will in one generation, we must establish the second and third generations to fulfill it. In other words, we must become the protagonists of the belief that we will fulfill the will even by establishing a lineage.

The Mission of the Unification Church
<Summary of the Words> The enemy of the body is a temporary enemy, but the enemy of the heart is an eternal enemy. Jesus came to this earth to overcome the world of the body and establish the world of the heart.

Until the day of judgment comes, we must fight. The purpose of religion is to conquer the body. There are many weapons of the body in the world, but there are no weapons of the heart. Equipping the heart with weapons is the essence of religion.

The Unification Church is on God's side, so we must love what God loves. God loves heaven, humanity, and the earth. The purpose of salvation is to establish a world of love.

The heart wants to give all love to the body, God, and the entire universe. Therefore, the heart is a king over the body, and the commands of the heart are precious.

God wants to love humanity centered on humans and the earth. We must know God's will (desire), circumstances, and heart, and we must become one with God forever in the place we are in. The Unification Church aims to teach these three things. Until now, humanity has tried to understand God's will, circumstances, and heart but has not been able to. That is why the Unification Church aims to teach this. No matter how many times we may abandon our bodies, we cannot abandon God.

Adam and Eve are the objects of God's hope; they are the existence of God's highest circumstances, heart, and desire. Therefore, humanity does not need any circumstances, heart, or desire beyond that.

Satan cannot love humanity. If he loves, he must give freedom, but if freedom is given, humanity will return to God. That is why he leads humanity with threats.

Thus, humanity is an enemy before God and also an enemy before Satan. However, God has raised such humans as His servants. No matter how evil humanity is, it loves its own lineage, but Satan cannot even love his own lineage.

God's providence in the Old Testament was to raise humans, who could not even be servants of Satan, as His servants. He expanded the realm of servants centered on Abraham.

Jesus carried out the providence of salvation that could make people sons. Therefore, they can only go to paradise.

The reason Jesus could not speak to the Israelites about the heart (John 16:12) was that they were God's sons. The reason Jesus washed the feet of the disciples is also here. In this way, Jesus started from the position of a son by taking away all that God had blessed humanity as servants.

Thus, he had no place to be or eat. The period in which Jesus taught his disciples to live as servants was his three years of public life. Jesus tried to raise the disciples to the direct line, but they could not follow that. So he alone established the way of being a son and built paradise.

After that, the 2,000 years of history was the foundation laid by Jesus and the Holy Spirit to establish direct children. Therefore, Christianity remains within the realm of the providence of salvation for sons. To raise them, the returning Jesus must fulfill the will without dying on the cross.

If today's Christian believers cannot take responsibility, the returning Lord must bear the cross again. Only when Jesus returns and stands in a position to hold the wedding feast can he raise humans in the position of sons to the direct line. When Jesus gives birth to children, those children (Christian believers) can stand in the position of brides.

If humanity had not fallen, they would have become true children of God, forming true couples and becoming true parents. Therefore, the ultimate purpose of humanity is to find true parents, pass through the position of sons, and advance to the position of direct children to form brides and grooms. The purpose of the returning Lord is also to lead humanity to such a position and establish them as His representatives.

The Unification Church has brought humanity from being servants to sons, and from sons to children, leading them to the standard of being blessed.

For God to establish humans as servants, He must become a servant of servants Himself. God, who gave Jesus to the cross, stood in a position more sorrowful than Jesus. Therefore, one must not only understand Jesus' heart but also understand God's heart.

Now is the time for the spiritual world to come to find humanity. That is why even those who do not pray are being dealt with. However, even though God has been working for 6,000 years, humanity has only become sons (4,000 years as servants, 2,000 years as sons). Can we raise them to the position of brides in a short time?

What Jesus taught through symbols and parables was because humanity was in the position of servants. That is why he could not teach the heart of parents.

I must fulfill the will of God that has not been achieved from all the saints of history to Jesus. Adam, Noah, Abraham, and others did not fully understand God's will. That is why they could not resolve God's grievances. Now you must understand God's heart and resolve His grievances. Originally, Adam should have remained without falling.

You must know the reasons for the mistakes of Adam, Noah, and Abraham and repent in their place. The mission of the Unification Church is to create such people. Such people can become the representatives of true parents and can enter heaven without the redemption of Jesus. The teacher intends to create such people within three years.

The teacher also went through this process starting from the path of servants. To escape the position of God's enemy, one must advance to the position of giving birth to good children.

To become a son, there must be a servant. Jesus was in the position of a servant. To become children, there must be sons.

To become good parents, there must be good children. Only after establishing a set of sons who can be blessed can one give birth to children.

This tour is the last of the public tours for the three-year period. In the future, God will not reprimand even if the tour is not conducted directly.

Live and fight to achieve the world of joy and glory
<Summary of the Words> The original purpose of God in creating creatures was to enjoy joy and glory. However, due to human mistakes, unwanted sorrow and complications have arisen. Thus, God has been working hard until now without achieving the purpose of creation, leaving it as a wish.

The reason Jesus was sorrowful
All creatures created from the first day to the sixth day were made for God to feel joy. In particular, humans created on the sixth day were the substantial object created to feel greater joy.

But why has God's purpose of creation remained as a historical grievance? Everyone would answer that it is due to the mistakes of the human ancestors, Adam and Eve. Thus, all the sorrows of history began not because of God but because of humanity.

For 4,000 years, God has never been able to be in a state of joy and glory, fighting against Satan. The Messiah Jesus, who came as the substantial being God had hoped for and to whom joy and glory should be given, was not recognized by anyone as the fruition of 4,000 years of history, the embodiment of glory and hope. Jesus was the embodiment of joy and glory before God, but on earth, he became the embodiment of sorrow, spending over 30 years of his life in sorrow.

Jesus, who came as the embodiment of glory and joy, should have revealed joy in his life, but he could not, so how great must the sorrow of Jesus and God have been? After 4,000 years of darkness due to the fall, God sent Jesus, but he again walked the path of sorrowful death, so how great must God's sorrow have been? We must understand that God had to taste a second great sorrow.

Jesus, who could not reveal God's glory and joy on this earth, is...
I felt a greater sorrow in not being able to fulfill God's desire to be in glory and joy than in not being able to establish my own face before Him. We must understand that the tip of that unspeakable sorrow pierced the heart of Jesus. Therefore, even before Jesus actually felt the pain of carrying the cross, He already experienced the inner pain of the cross.

After countless crowds faded away like a dream, the sorrow of not being able to inform even His disciples of the sad circumstances that required Him to go to the Garden of Gethsemane was immense. Imagine the heart of Jesus, who worried about leaving sorrow behind before the Father. His footsteps carrying the cross were the most painful steps. We must understand the heart of Jesus as He went to the Garden of Gethsemane, praying while thinking of God's pain internally and the pain of the saints externally. 

Furthermore, we must recognize that when Jesus cried out, "Father!" it was a plea that reflected God's heart of creation, His own heart of responsibility, and God's anxious heart worrying about the future. "Abba, Father! If it is possible, let this cup pass from me." This was not to avoid His own pain, but a fervent prayer asking that if it were possible, He could avoid this ordeal so that the fulfillment of God's purpose could be achieved through Him.

What greater circumstances could there be than this? Knowing the historical labor of God, Jesus cried out, "Abba, Father..." and we must understand that He was more miserable and tormented than anyone else. You must understand the heart of Jesus, who pleaded so earnestly because thousands of years of struggle and the providence of salvation remained.

There was no joy in Jesus' life. Even the miracle of the five loaves and two fish did not bring joy. Jesus' disciples also failed to become beings of hope and glory. Just as Jesus had to become the embodiment of joy and glory before God, His disciples also needed to become the embodiment of joy and glory before Jesus. However, they could not become such embodiments. Therefore, Jesus wanted to leave His intentions in their hearts but could not.

Even the records of the Bible show that Jesus did not go in joy and glory. He was born in sorrow and suffering, lived in sorrow and suffering, and departed in sorrow and suffering. If He had come in sorrow but left in joy and glory, He would have become the embodiment of glory, but because He came with hope and joy yet could not fulfill His purpose, that purpose remains as hope until now.

The Correct Attitude of Faith

Today, we believe in the suffering Jesus. The 30 years spent in the household of Joseph were also a life of suffering; thus, Jesus lived a life of suffering both inside and out. 

Why did the twelve apostles and countless crowds follow Jesus? They followed Him for their own glory, looking for glory on earth. However, when that did not happen, they ultimately could not unite and ended up dividing.

If the disciples had been aware of the inner and outer pains Jesus was suffering, He would have shared His pain with them. However, because He could not do so, most people today also do not know of Jesus' suffering. Thus, they cannot know of Jesus' glory even more.

For Jesus, the visible pain was not the issue. The issue was fulfilling God's desire, so Jesus faced everything with that standard. He approached the table and the place to lie down, anticipating a day of desire.

In the end, the question is whether you have truly become the bride or disciple that Jesus desires. Can you qualify to be such a person? 

Two thousand years ago, Jesus walked the path of Golgotha, bearing the pain of both inner and outer suffering without being able to express His heart of hope. He did not go with joy and satisfaction but with sorrow and pain. Jesus could not release the pain of His heart on this earth. He could not leave behind glory, nor could He leave behind the pain of His heart. Nevertheless, the saints follow the path of Golgotha to inherit the sorrow and pain that Jesus endured when He left. The path of faith is precisely such a path.

Since the physical path of Golgotha still remains, the Holy Spirit is suffering. Therefore, a time will come when, centered on humanity, we can settle the history of sin, and it is the desire of Jesus and the Holy Spirit to inform the saints of the pain Jesus endured, which He could not express to His disciples.

If God called Jesus, who could not fulfill His desire, He must have called Him with a sense of regret.

Jesus has been praying until today. The Holy Spirit is also praying here on earth. This is because both Jesus and the Holy Spirit must take responsibility for human sin and establish a world of joy and glory.

Jesus praying in paradise is never at ease. It is because He has not become the Son of Glory. The same goes for the Holy Spirit. Jesus has continued to live a life of the cross for 2,000 years since His death, not only during His 30 years of life. 

The prayer, "Abba, Father!" has continued not only at that time but for 2,000 years in paradise. If Jesus is like this, so is the Holy Spirit.

Christians ask God for joy and glory from the day they believe. They seek not the joy and glory of this earth but those of the next world. They only seek to enjoy joy and glory, unaware that there is a path of the cross behind it.

So, what is the reason you have gathered here today? Like them, you will not demand the opposite of joy, happiness, and glory. However, neither God, Jesus, nor the Holy Spirit has experienced joy and glory. Such concepts exist, but they have not yet been realized. Therefore, it is impossible to say, "Give me joy and glory, and let the sorrow and pain belong to the Father."

God has not experienced the joy and glory since creation, so humans on earth cannot possess them first. In the human world, children cannot possess the inheritance before their parents. Likewise, we humans cannot possess the joy and glory that the Trinity has not experienced. Therefore, we must inherit the cross before inheriting glory and must inherit death before inheriting a blessed life. This is the heritage that Christians must inherit.

Even in paradise, it is only joyful if God is pleased, and it is joyful if Jesus is pleased. If Jesus is praying, we cannot be joyful. First, we must free Jesus from His suffering while He prays. Is not Jesus fighting through prayer? God, Jesus, and the Holy Spirit are all pleading for the end times to come. They are waiting to settle the cross and welcome the day of joy and glory.

The Position of Humanity

Everyone hopes that the pain of life will pass, but it will not pass until the pain of Jesus and the Holy Spirit passes. The door of joy has not yet been opened before Jesus.

You fight to be liberated from your personal pain, but Jesus and the Holy Spirit are fighting for the entire world, the spiritual world, and the physical world. When will that pain cease? It is the heart of Jesus that can only weep. Yet, feeling responsible, Jesus cannot cry. Who understood the heart of Jesus, who had to walk the path of death with His disciples and Israel behind Him, unable to weep? Before we can have glory or happiness, we must first free Jesus, who is in pain.

Do not believe from a comfortable place. You must believe from the place of the cross. If it seems acceptable to believe from a comfortable place, why would God or Jesus still be in such a place? Will you believe like Peter or the other disciples at that time? While Jesus was praying His final prayer in the Garden of Gethsemane, they were sleeping. Is that believing in Jesus? To believe in Jesus, you must believe from the place where the cross and life and death intersect.

Just because there are many Christians does not mean that the tradition is inherited. The tradition of Christianity has been inherited through a few who fought, died, and represented the world, just as Moses represented the Israelite nation.

If you endure to the end, there will surely come a time when you will have no relationship with the power of death. God cannot say to Jesus, "Do not pray, but live eternally in my throne." It is a restoration history; therefore, first, there must be True Parents, second, True Children, third, True Siblings, and fourth, True Couples. Only then can we finally enjoy glory and joy.

Since the fall, has there been anyone who could say to God, "Oh, my beloved"? The angels did not sing out of joy when they saw Jesus lying in a manger. How can it be that the Prince of Heaven, who had been awaited for 4,000 years, was laid in a manger? A child can walk freely where their parents' inheritance is. But did Jesus walk freely on the earth created by His Father? Why did He have to be wrapped in swaddling clothes and laid in a manger?

Due to the fall of the first human ancestors, Adam and Eve, all humans could not become True Parents, True Children, True Siblings, or True Couples. They became the children of Satan, the siblings of Satan, and the couples of Satan. This applies to everyone, regardless of gender.

If the needle of a compass points north and south, a stronger force than the compass's power is needed to turn it in the opposite direction. Even though there was a fall, like the needle of the compass pointing north and south, our conscience is directed toward God.

Satan is the enemy of God. You are neither a child of God nor a child of Satan. There is a great enemy between heaven and earth, and that is Satan. From God's perspective, Satan is an adulterer.

If Adam had completed his mission, he would have established the temple of God and become the embodiment of God. If Adam and Eve had become one as a couple, Eve would have become the wife who embodies God. If that had happened, they could have inherited God's lineage. However, like a servant who violated the daughter of a wealthy family, Satan took away Eve, who was God's daughter.

Originally, it was a principle that God should be the parent of humanity, but Satan established a blood relationship with humanity and positioned himself as the parent first. It turns out that all humans are children of Satan, who is the enemy of God.

However, Satan cannot say, "These are my children." Deep within humanity lies a conscience that seeks to return to God. Unable to give up on such humans, Satan constantly threatens them. Although Satan has established a blood relationship with humanity, he does not grant them freedom. If he gives them freedom, they will return to God. Therefore, Satan always threatens and controls humanity, saying, "If you go, I will kill you." You cannot even become a servant of Satan.

If humanity had not fallen and had established a loving relationship with God as the True Children of True Parents, that relationship could not have been severed by anyone. Although the body of humanity is connected to Satan, the heart seeks to return to God. Once a relationship is established with God, no one can sever it. However, since a relationship has been established with Satan, that relationship must be severed.

Satan treats humanity as enemies. Humanity cannot even become servants of Satan. The history of making such humans into servants of God was the Old Testament era. Here, we aim to elevate servants to adopted children, adopted children to direct descendants, descendants to siblings, and siblings to brides and grooms, leading them to the position of True Parents. Since we have lost the family centered on God, restoring it is the purpose of restoration. Introducing Jesus into the position of True Parents is the Feast of the Lamb.

Jesus, who continues to pray even in paradise, has made beings who cannot even become servants of Satan into servants of God, so fallen humanity would have no regrets even if they died as servants of God. However, God wishes to elevate such humans to establish a blood relationship with True Parents. The day that relationship is established is the end time. Do you know what deceiving the people means? Those who say that heaven and earth will disappear in the last days are the deceivers.

Where are the True Children, True Siblings, and True Couples? Where are those who have reached the position of True Parents? If such families exist, they become God's direct descendants.

If Jesus had fulfilled His purpose on earth, there would have been no physical Golgotha or spiritual Golgotha. However, because Jesus could not fulfill His purpose, there exists a spiritual Golgotha in the spiritual world and a physical Golgotha on earth. Therefore, when humans die, they must go to the spiritual world and undergo another trial. They must be tested on how they lived on earth. In the spiritual world, paradise is the forefront, and on earth, your physical body is the forefront.

The path of restoration cannot be smooth. As it passes through the first, second, and third generations, it becomes heavier. You are the embodiment of the total sum of the bloodline sins of 6,000 years. You are the exhibition of 6,000 years of sin. Each of your cells is intertwined with 6,000 years of sin. To unravel this, historical repentance is necessary.

What did Jesus do during His 30 years of preparation? He repented of historical sins. He repented and resolved all historical mistakes and historical diseases to become the historical Savior. The tearing of the temple veil signifies that the saints were elevated due to Jesus' repentance.

Next, He repented of the sins of the era. When the altar established around the Jewish temple is referred to as Israel, it was necessary to repent of the sins of the era. Therefore, Jesus prayed for them, saying, "Do not hold their sins against them," taking responsibility for their sins. After that, He repented of future sins. Only then can He become the Messiah. Jesus repented to settle historical and era-specific sins and fought for the future.

But where did such Jesus go? By dying, His merits of historical repentance, merits of era-specific repentance, and merits of fighting for the future were all nullified. That is why Jesus has been praying since His resurrection. He is praying and working to establish a standard that can settle historical, era-specific, and future sins in paradise. The Jesus who carried the physical cross is now carrying the spiritual cross. Therefore, you must become someone who says, "I will drive out the Satan and sins that you wish to expel."

Jesus repented of all historical sins, such as Cain's sin, the sins of Noah's family, and Moses' mistakes, throughout His 30 years of life, but since that was undone, it must be repented again to become the bride. Even if you say, "These guys..." about your ancestors, they must be able to respond, "Yes, that is correct," to survive in place of Adam, Noah, and Moses.

The sweat, tears, and blood that Jesus shed were not only for that time or that generation but were meant to allow the entire world to live through 4,000 years of history. We must understand how Jesus prayed with blood in the Garden of Gethsemane and continues to pray even in paradise. We must understand His heart and repent.

The world of glory and joy that God desires has not been realized. Where and how should you go? Heaven is not reached by flying but through the path of Golgotha. Look at world history. At that time, the historical cross of this earth will unfold.
Yes. We must fight against Satan in the spiritual world as well.
