The Significance of the Holy Land Separation and the Three-Year Course
<Summary of the Message> Among the members, create opportunities for contact by forming a trinity. The places where members meet should be sanctified and set as a standard for the restoration of all things. Thus, family members passing through the area can stop by to pray and leave. In this way, they should develop an interest in the sanctified area and cultivate the custom of visiting the holy land.

Due to the stimulation of the value of all things, they will come to feel their own value. The reason the Israelite nation fell was that they lost their attachment to the blessed things.

Complete the sanctification of the holy land by the lunar month of August. Even in places without members, sanctification should be done, and evangelism should be conducted to secure the sanctified places.

Sanctify a piece of land of at least eight paces in all directions at 0:30 AM. By the 10th of the lunar month of September (the date has been changed again), decide and sanctify the holy lands of each region. Just as Abraham wanted to be buried in the sanctified land of his body, in the past, the holy fire could not be sprinkled outside.

The three-year course is a period for the teacher to lay the foundation for fulfilling the national mission. This period is for laying the heavenly foundation.

Members must cooperate for this. This three-year period is one with many hardships. Because of this period, a standard for family restoration has been established for the members. 

Due to this condition, they have been able to enter the realm of the benefits of tribal restoration. 

From now on, blessed members must support the teacher to establish a global standard. Blessed individuals must enable local leaders and district leaders to emerge as global pioneers.

Only after the teacher has fulfilled this global mission can a position be established. Blessed members must walk the path of tribal restoration while also cooperating in the teacher's establishment of a global restoration standard.

After the three-year period ends, each of you must restore your own tribe. That time will come. In this way, the restored tribes can combine to restore a nation.

During this three-year period, those with faithful children will have a global standard. A tradition of supporting the teacher must be established. However, because this has not been established, you find yourselves in the same position as the teacher. Originally, to receive blessings, one must offer what their three generations possess. Marriage must also be based on the support of these three generations. Receiving support from the teacher is something to be ashamed of.

The offerings presented before God are holy things, even if they become moldy. Blessed families are offerings. Therefore, there should be no complaints. If Isaac had complained, he would not have become an offering.

You must create inheritable children to find rest. Our ancestors in the spirit world have a heart connection that is at least one-third established. Therefore, evangelism becomes easier. Additionally, because there is a bloodline connection, establishing the reality becomes easier.

Blessings allow for the emergence of a new Israel. If one Abel-type and one Cain-type are established in each of the 36 families, it becomes 72 families.

If we represent the vertical history horizontally, we can draw the following diagram.

<Diagram:012049.jpg>
Even in the same era, a person with a low spirit cannot ascend from A to B in one leap; they must ascend from A to A', A'', A''', and so on to B'. Thus, they must go through the stages of A, A', A'', and so on. This is the reason to follow Abel.

Unification begins in the heart. Heart-centered unity arises from a miserable position. Therefore, one must intentionally walk the path of hardship. The path of hardship cannot be slandered by either God or Satan.

Only those who receive the sympathy of the poor can become solid leaders. The world of communism also suffers greatly, which is why God cannot punish them. That is why they also develop.

You must become someone whom God loves, someone whom family members sympathize with, or someone whom all things rejoice in; you must be one of these three.

When leading a gathering, start the message from the perspective of the most miserable person. When touring, you must first visit the places that are the least successful.

Strengthen the tour organization and make sure to rotate through the areas, including the districts, even if it is just for a day. Within three years, the mission proclaimed by the teacher must be fulfilled.

8)
The Responsibility of Blessed Families
<Summary of the Message> The members' hearts regarding blessings are lacking. The teacher chose the tribes to entrust them with a national mission while the teacher undertakes the mission of global restoration.

During the three-year period, one must surpass the standard of Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob. Marrying 72 pairs this year was excessive. There are only a few pairs that I find suitable.

The valley of death must be filled with the children of God. This is because God's children created that valley. Therefore, our members must fill it, which requires hardship.

Since we cannot fill it by killing everyone, we must at least cut off one limb at a time to fill it. Thus, sacrifice is necessary. Those who followed the teacher were the first to sacrifice. Only then can those who come in the future sacrifice without complaint.

I have never taken a nap until now. I had to sit in meditation all day.

You must establish a heavenly tradition. You must establish it even if it requires blood, sweat, and tears. If you cannot establish it yourself, you must do so through your children.

If you make a mistake, you can only become a servant. To work and leave is the role of a servant. A person who only bears witness to me is in the position of a servant. If you work from a position that is seen as bad in God's eyes, you will be broken. Such churches will be broken, and such nations will be broken.

Because God blessed the Israelite nation, He punished them when they could not take responsibility. An evangelist is a representative of the teacher. Therefore, you must walk the path of the tribe that seeks the ideology in front, blessed brothers on the sides, the nation above, and the individual below.

Those who speak carelessly will inevitably face scrutiny. This is because you received blessings after making a vow. Since you have been blessed, you will no longer interfere. If even one blessed person is willing to follow the will, they can emerge.

To the grandmothers entrusted with the mission of prayer, direct interference is made. However, you must not tread on the teacher's lifestyle as it is. You cannot freely go to the theater either.

After this period, a spiritual age will come.

What is different before and after the fall? The heart is different. There must be an ideology accompanied by the heart and a body accompanied by the heart. After a certain period, a time of reorganization will come. Children must also receive blessings again.

You must be able to regret not conveying God's will with these eyes and this body.

As a blessed person, you should feel ashamed of leaving words before God. What God desires is to move centered around the teacher. You must be a shadow.

There are symbolic blessings and substantial blessings. The teacher does not change, but you do.

The teacher does not sympathize with the Moon family. If something goes wrong, it can involve even the ancestors.

The teacher travels three thousand miles in a single night. The teacher is unable to say what needs to be said. What will the satans fear? There was a time when angels accompanied the teacher.

Protect your body. To do this, no one can interfere before the teacher gives orders. No one can violate the heavenly bloodline. No one can turn back the heart of heaven. We must absolutely keep these three conditions.

From now on, the three must unite. If there are no children, you must establish an adopted child. In the future, collective living must be practiced. You must receive blessings from a position where you can receive sympathy.

When you step into a public position for the tour, you cannot even think about the baby. The teacher lives to create a new history.

It is frustrating to have lost the clothes worn in prison.

What materials do you have to hold your children and leave a will? You cannot lie to your children, so you must reorganize your inner life. If each cannot do it, I will try to do it.

The teacher becomes serious when thinking about the impending death at any moment. Thinking about fulfilling the remaining mission within a limited time... 

9)
Become the Fruit of History
<Summary of the Message> The students gathered here are young people who have come together from churches across the nation. To speak to the youth, the teacher must also become young. To what extent should one become young? You would wish for the teacher to be the same age and even share the same birthday as you. The teacher desires to become that young. Right now, your age is similar to the age at which the teacher sought this meaning.

You have gathered today to attend this assembly, and each of you likely came with a multitude of thoughts. Although many people have come, how many have come with a sincere heart? How many will leave with a sincere heart?

God, the center of the world and history
So, to whom will the teacher speak? Without a doubt, it will be to those who have come with a sincere heart. It is the responsibility and mission of a leader to create such sincere individuals, even if it requires force.

One must not act recklessly. One must become someone who can act for the whole.

Today, this 30 million nation, and indeed all humanity, and furthermore, God, what kind of person are they waiting for? Even a child can answer the same. They are waiting for a historical fruit-bearing individual.

So, what position do you find yourselves in? Let's see. What are you doing? You are living. Among people, some live merely to eat, others think, and some speak to spread a certain ideology, while others bravely fight to put that ideology into practice. If all these actions are done solely for oneself, one cannot escape historical judgment.

Then, what kind of person lives for heaven and earth? How should one live, speak, and act? Who is more precious: the person who lives for themselves or the one who lives for their family, nation, or even the world? It is undeniable that the person who lives for a greater cause is the more precious one.

The history of the world today is connected to the One who created it. Therefore, no matter how unworthy a person may be, they are a global figure, and you and I are all individuals with a global perspective.

So, for whom should we live? We should live for those who strive to make heaven and earth our own. We should live for those who think of the highest ideals that God desires.

God is the One who practices through words and character, and He came for the universe. Moreover, God is absolute in both words and practice. When has God ever spoken and practiced? The more chaotic the environment, the more pitiful God is.

Until now, there has been no one who lives such a life and practices such words. To create such individuals and to allow them to live in the eternal ideal world, He sent the first person of hope, who is the Messiah.

This world belongs to humanity. However, materialism is based on economic views and values a material-centered world. But democracy centers on the person itself. Communism must first seek the person. In this sense, democracy is a step ahead of communism. However, within this democracy, there remains the task of moving from a human-centered approach to a God-centered one. In other words, we must elevate ourselves to a world where we live with God.

God is not merely the God of the Vatican or Catholicism. God is the God of world religions and the God of humanity. The world is gradually being organized into the ideal world that God desires. Therefore, God cannot be confined to the feudal Vatican or Catholicism. The world must inevitably become one, and it will, because that is what God desires.

The future era is the era of the heart
God is first looking for one person who can represent the world. Why did He destroy the seven nations of Canaan? It was because they did not have the foundation for forming a nation for God, and they were judged from a global perspective. Nationalistic thoughts will inevitably be broken when it comes to serving the world. The question is whether one can pass through the gates of judgment in such a situation. God wants to create those who can say, "God's heart is also mine." Thus, He has led individuals, families, and nations through suffering to a global position.

Today's history is in a position similar to that of a woman in labor. Modern civilization is said to be the product of the Renaissance, but from now on, the heart will become the issue. God and we are one. Furthermore, from God's perspective, the world is also one. Borders are unnecessary. From God's perspective, there is only one world. Borders are all enemies. Who drew the lines?

So, what kind of value does the person God desires possess? Whose is this cup (placed on the desk)? It belongs to the Creator and to humanity. All things also hope to participate in that value and are still groaning. Those who violate this should be judged. Whose is that mountain? Is it Mr. Kim's? No, it belongs only to God.

You must live with the mindset that the world is yours. That is why you are called the embodiment of hope and the lighthouse of hope. You are the holy princes who will inherit heaven and earth. But are you selling yourselves for a piece of bread? That cannot be. You must restore human nature and recognize your inherent value, establishing all relationships according to the laws of heaven and earth, connecting reality and the future. Such a person is the one whom the nation hopes for, the one whom 3 billion people hope for, and the one whom all spirits in the spirit world hope for. 

This world is mine, and the God who created this universe is also mine. A person who can do this is someone who cannot be exchanged for all of Korea, America, or even the 3 billion people of the world. Where is such a person?

You must have this sense of ownership, saying that the world is mine and the earth is mine. It is lamentable that I have wandered through the valley of darkness. Such a person must die. I am now a person who is searching for my original self, a person whom God is seeking, and if just 100,000 young people who are seeking the nation of hope come together, they can dominate the world. You must become a young person who longs for the nation of hope. What did you intend to do? How did you plan to live?

We must transcend national sentiments. We must not discriminate between black and white. Rather, those who think themselves superior will be judged. Is the son of a wealthy family perfect while the disabled child scores zero? No.

The democratic camp must go to Africa and share treasures, sharing blood and flesh. If one does not become a brother who seeks the lost sibling, they will break apart. The reason communism is expanding today is that they still have some semblance of the form in which God seeks to save the pitiful.

Before establishing the ties of God's love on this earth, we must not live in complacency.

History is moving from the age of material distribution and human distribution to the age of heart distribution. For a child to inherit their parent's wealth, they must receive their parent's love. Until then, they cannot have inheritance rights.

First, there will be an age of material blessings, followed by an age of human blessings, and then a heart-centered age of blessings focused on God.

However, for the righteous, material blessings are not given, and they are pushed toward the final heart to inherit. The steps taken by religious individuals centered on theology until now have been steps to inherit God's heart.

Whenever anything is given, it must be given with the heart of a parent who wants to give more. It must be given with feeling. It should not be given as mere shells.

Now is the age of brothers. It is also the age of brotherly societies and nations. Therefore, the time has come for Cain and Abel, who are fighting, to unite.

What kind of person does God seek? God wants to say, "I want to give you something." Who can do that? God first wants to give to the pitiful. Among the pitiful, those who cultivate the way are the most pitiful. Therefore, they should be given first. And when that righteous person says thank you and now no longer needs it, they should give it to others, and that is how it should continue.

You must become a person who can remain in the universe.

In this historical time, how should we lead people? The world is mine. You must become someone who thinks, speaks, and acts with the new world in mind. Until now, you have lived for yourself, and at best, for your parents and siblings. But that can no longer be the case.

So, what kind of person should you become? You must become someone who lives for the world, for God. Even in eating, humans are inferior to all things. All things are groaning, longing for a day of reconciliation. They desire a person who can truly remain in the universe...

If there is a Creator, you must become a person needed by that Creator in the past, present, and future. Thus, you must lead people to God. The "I" being spoken of here and all of you present must work for such a person.

In the world of the heart, everyone is equal. In heaven, the elderly are treated as parents, humanity is treated as one family, and all men and women are treated as brothers. Heaven is an expanded world of family, a world of brotherhood.

The universe continues to revolve along its orbit, even if we are dozing off. If no one is watching and you act recklessly, you will perish. The less you are seen, the better you must act.

Even when others give me something, I must have the heart of a parent, saying I am satisfied with this. Please give for the world. God does not give leftovers. Those who give leftovers cannot become great people.

To fulfill God's will, one must also have a revolutionary spirit. Before the will, before God, one must become the best person.

We must go. It is our destiny to go. So, what should we do now? When you step outside, will you forget your vows? That cannot be. You must not change even after a thousand years. God has desired to see such a being, but until now, those who have appeared on this earth have not become such beings. They are acting in ways that God has not even imagined.

The Israelite people and God have come through bloodlines. God is a pitiful being. He has never stood in a place of glory, but has fought through a place of despair, being oppressed and cursed. God bears the historical scars of arrows. The history of the chosen people is made up of blood and death.

Even when individuals perish, there were heirs of families; when families perish, there were heirs of nations; and when nations perish, there were heirs of the world. Yet God still cannot escape His miserable state.

That is why God is crying out with both hands raised. Is there no warrior to fight for humanity, for God? From the perspective of Jesus, we must fulfill the destiny that remains before us without dying. We must achieve this for our ancestors who have passed away, for ourselves, and for our descendants. If it is difficult to repay the grievances of individuals, how easy will it be to repay the grievances of history and humanity?

God is sorrowful. The hopes of Noah built upon 120 years, or even 1,600 years, have collapsed, and after another 400 years, Abraham failed, and then Moses made mistakes... We must become warriors who will take responsibility for all of this and fulfill God's will.

Now is the time to charge toward the enemy, to charge toward the enemy camp. Do you understand? Noah, Abraham, Moses, and Jesus were all forsaken by their families. If the Father comes to this land, let us take responsibility. Everything is within us. This society, this nation, this world has become this way because of us. If we shed tears for God, we will not perish.

God is the one who gives first, who is beaten and robbed. You must be the same. God's miserable providence is also because of us. We must understand God's historical heart, which wants to say, "I want to speak like you and work like you." God does not forget and waits. Think about when you can participate in God's providence of restoration. You must find a stage of life where you can live with God. And you must find a way to think, speak, and act like God.

God is everything; it is the life of the cross and the way of the cross. Therefore, we have the responsibility to represent God. Walk the path of the cross. Walk the path of death. Since we have sown with the cross, we must reap with tears and wailing. Those who wish to live will die, and those who wish to die will live. Living for a single village means living on behalf of 3 billion humanity.

The mission of those established before God's will
We must think about the time when we can live even for an hour like God and work for that time; this is our mission established before the Father. We must go to the cross. The teacher has not yet grown weary. Moreover, there is no difficult path that cannot be walked further. Personally, I have many enemies, but I do not hate any of them. First, we must repay the grievances of the world.

Today’s era is the global Canaan restoration era. The Israelite people during Moses' time did not know themselves. Their longing for the promised land of Canaan was weak, and they did not recognize their leader. Thus, they could not help but perish. Throughout history, whenever such beings existed, they have never survived. They all perished, and only those under 20 remained. Even if there were 600,000 men, could they have succeeded? Would they have been able to? Even if they all surrendered, you must not surrender. The slaughter of 600,000 Israelites was the price they paid for their inability to take responsibility.

We must unite.

When you look at your teacher, from what position do you look? "Make me a chosen people." You must find a leader who will drive you even if it means hitting you, a leader who will push you even if it means striking you with a sword. If Moses had taken up a sword to drive the Israelite people, even if 100,000 had died, 600,000 would not have perished.

No matter what ideological trials come to us, it is not a problem. We must cast aside anything that hinders our path. We must hope that our leader will pull us along. If we do not go, we will perish. Therefore, we must fulfill the mission of global Canaan restoration by any means necessary. This mission rests on the shoulders of us, the Unification Church members. If we do not go, we need a leader who will make us go, even if it means hitting us. We just need to go. Only then can we become historical victors, era-leading vanguards, and future pioneers.
No one can set the standard of character. If one falls short compared to that person (the Messiah), they are a less fortunate individual. If a new world is to come, there must be a center to govern it, and this person is the Lord of the Second Advent spoken of in Christianity.  
October 9, 1962 (Tuesday), Former Headquarters Church.  
* This message was given during the national district leaders' meeting and has been organized from the notes of former chairman Yoo Hyo-won. The title was added by the editor.  
60   Conscience is the Key to the Gates of Heaven.  
You must meet God, who serves as the standard figure. You must meet God, who appears through the subject and forms a connection with you.  
A true person of character lives not just for their family, society, or nation, but for God, heaven, and earth. They live for God, who governs humanity and the earth. Therefore, while you should live your life in your family, your heart must live for the cosmos. You must move from the stage of wanting to serve God to the stage of actually living for God.  
A person of character emerges through the Absolute Being. Conscience becomes happy when it establishes absolute subjects and relative standards and exchanges with them.  
At the time of judgment, a new world will appear, and all nations will need to prepare for that world. Those who can remain at that time will be the citizens of that nation.  
At the end of days, the main character who will govern the world will appear, and then God, who establishes this main character, will reveal Himself.  
You have come here to seek a new world at this end time. The path we are taking is a difficult one where good families go hungry, and good nations go hungry.  
However, if there is someone you want to give to, serve, and care for, even after giving and giving again, that person is the happiest person.  
If a path that takes ten years can be traveled in five years, then that path should be chosen. Conscience drives you to travel a path that would normally take ten years in ten hours, even if it means punishing the body. Conscience does not lead to my ruin. Rather, it makes me bow my head before those who do good.  
11)  
Suffering and Blessing  
<Summary of the Message> The blessed are Abel before the world. Therefore, when offering sacrifices, one must put in more sincerity than anyone else.  
Our suffering is for the sake of providing a refuge for the people of the world. Do not die; rather, suffer.  
Listening to Elder Jang makes me feel ashamed. It is because I should have blessed even more significant family members. The blessing of 72 families was given because there was a standard that endured hardship for the purpose. Serving the purpose is sorrowful yet joyful, but serving oneself is joyful yet sorrowful.  
What the teacher wants to say in his will is simply to suffer.  
When sending spies to the land of Canaan, the best representatives would have been sent. The teacher also intends to send smart individuals to the North.  
If someone who is to receive five matches ten, then those five will be repaid by God. Therefore, Christianity must become a religion of sacrifice.  
I fear that because of the blessed families, other family members may not be able to speak. Therefore, families must live a life of restraint.  
One must become someone whom the nation can sympathize with. Let us not incur emotional debts. Although six million people of the Israelite nation died, they did not receive blessings.  
This path is one that the teacher established with the determination of life and death. It was not established based on human-centered desires. The teacher knows that there is a purpose to establish more than three pairs within a nation.  
You must become a heart-centered patriarch. You must walk this path even if it means death. Do you think Jesus died in vain? The teacher is doing this work despite his painful body.  
Those who will be added to the earth will never die. Perhaps those who are under conditions of indemnity may not. When a blessed person hears the word, a feeling of resentment against Satan must rise.  
The teacher intends to sit anywhere. Have you made a place for the teacher to sit in a clean place?  
I love Yejin, but I am thinking of the day I must leave her behind. When Abraham was about to kill Isaac, Isaac did not resist, and that is commendable. Is there any need to advise a filial son two or three times? God spoke to Noah only once.  
Many incidents must be caused. However, do not leave behind what cannot be borne like Jesus. Whatever it may be, it must be resolved.  
The members in Seoul must strive to know the words the teacher spoke in the provinces before anyone else.  
12)  
Become a Value-Driven Fruitful Entity  
<Summary of the Message> You are now about to leave for your hometowns. The church that sends you and heaven have more worries than you do as you depart. This is because if you make a mistake, your personal mistake becomes a criminal act before the nation and heaven. Therefore, I hope you will become meaningful individuals before historical accomplishments as you initially resolved.  
Efforts and Completion and Value  
This year's slogan is to become someone who can show and boast. The words you have heard and the firm resolutions may gradually weaken. When the heart for the purpose becomes faint, you must remember the resolution to become someone who can show and boast.  
We must abandon everything centered on ourselves. Everything centered on oneself is false. We have lost God, the true world, the true nation, and the true family; thus, we must seek them again.  
In spring, the sunlight rising in the eastern sky becomes warmer, and all things prepare to reveal their value of existence from deep within the earth, wanting to appear in a proud manner in the new heaven and earth.  
October 19, 1962 (Friday), Former Headquarters Church.  
* This message was given as an encouragement speech at the 13th National Evangelist Training Conference graduation ceremony and has been organized from the publication <Seonghwa>, No. 21 (November 1, 1962).  
64   Become a Value-Driven Fruitful Entity  
Your completed form will manifest according to how much effort you have made for completion. After a year, you will show the growth corresponding to that year. Even a blade of grass, or trees like acacia, willow, or pine, will grow accordingly after a certain period and respond to the Creator's demands.  
In this training session, you have demonstrated how valuable your existence is through your training life. Now, how much you absorb of what God has provided depends on your efforts. Therefore, you must leave something before God and repay Him.  
What do you have in your heart? When you have a lively form like spring, how much of the essence of spring can you absorb? Everything depends on yourself. How much can your hands absorb, and how much can your feet gather during the harvest season? What is within your organs? What responsibilities do your limbs hold? Even if you do not wish to, remember that you are connected to the eternal world behind you.  
What can you show and what do you have to boast about? What are your eyes and feet doing in this relationship?  
Even if you try to escape this relationship and distance yourself, this relationship will define you as good or evil. In whatever relationship, all things in the universe are mobilized, and our lives and hearts are continuously moving within that relationship. Even if I rest, everything in the universe continues to move. God has placed us humans in this relationship and wishes for us to become a value-driven fruitful entity centered on this relationship.  
So, how long must we remain in this relationship? Until now, what have you been proud of? How trivial is your value? You, who lived for your own fullness! Humans are not inherently worthless beings. You have tried to boast of your frivolous self in the past. Now that you know you were created for the world, you must repay for that value. Under this goal, you must resolve to become someone who can show and boast.  
What have your hands done in the past? And what have your feet and body done? When you think about it, there is nothing in this body that you can present without shame. You would want to bury it all. However, whether good or bad, that is all part of my form. For the sake of this lump of flesh, I have given birth to the offspring of Satan and lived in the world of Satan. Until now, I have lived as a worthless being before God.  
What will you show and boast about?  
Now, what will you show? Your hands, feet, mouth, eyes, and nose are no longer what they used to be. Therefore, you must now become a splendid warrior. Each of you must return to your village and engage in a splendid struggle.  
In this end time, the world of good ideals and the world of evil ideals collide. Therefore, you must become those who can reveal the vitality that has not been shown until now.  
To do this, you must first engage in struggle. It is acceptable to be hit for the sake of good. Therefore, you must be able to bear all that others deem bad. Let us become warriors who show such a form.  
You must discard the rotten old self and go to the free universe to secure a rock-like position. After that, you must first organize your environment and then lead your village and town, expanding true activities. To struggle for one purpose, you must have a base.  
You must show the new spring light and become someone who can boast anew. You must discard the already dead self and start as a new warrior. You must become someone who can boast of your efforts and struggles before the world. From now on, you must start as a new self.  
You! Do you know what kind of history heaven and earth and humanity have gone through? Both heaven and earth have struggled through infinite sorrow, and humanity has also emerged from the valley of death.  
There is a bitter enemy who has made this happen. That enemy occupies not only nations and families but even my cells. We must reclaim the beautiful youth and young years we have lost due to this enemy.  
Behind us is God, the subject of goodness. This God calls us and is preparing a path to create a hope-filled entity.  
Centered on myself, there is above and below, front and back, left and right. Because I am not standing in my original position, heaven and earth have cried out. I am an existing being through the relationship of heaven and earth, and this universe exists to manifest God's form. Therefore, through this universe, I must realize my form. I must seek the universe that has been divided into the duality of the original nature.  
I must become a being that can show the entirety of heaven and earth. By showing heaven and showing earth, when I do not become a target of ridicule before Satan, I can naturally establish a dignified presence.  
I must be the one who shows the universe, the one who boasts on behalf of God, and thus become a valuable being.  
What does heaven want to show, and what does earth want to boast about? It is me, created through the emotional connection of heaven and earth. Heaven and earth want to find sons and daughters who can say, "Oh, my children!" Therefore, we must also want to boast before heaven and earth, saying that God the Father is my Father. I want to show my Father.  
You, at this moment, have no relationships in front and back, so the path ahead is daunting. You do not know how to live. You cannot even speak. Everything you learned was from Satan.  
People are pessimistic about the world. This is because they have not learned how to live. They have fallen and do not know their parents. Therefore, now you must recognize the relationship with the parents who can teach you about heaven and earth, above and below, front and back.  
The Father leads you from the front, and the Mother protects you from behind. This is something that can only be hoped for within the emotional relationship. When this happens, when I am sad, the parents will also be sad, and when I am lonely, the parents will also be lonely. When I am lonely and suffer to fulfill loyalty and filial piety, when I call upon my parents, the parents of heaven and earth will move with me, and God will protect me.  
Even if I am scorned, as long as I can introduce goodness for that village, that region, and that nation, it is enough. The goal is to find and serve the True Parents who lead me, and by living to serve the parents of tradition who have patiently sought me with eternal love, that person becomes a being who replaces the blood and flesh of the parents. You must learn the heart and lifestyle of the parents. Your individual existence is meant to show the True Parents.  
Finding Parents and Siblings  
To do this, you must find your left and right, that is, your siblings. If the two do not become one, you cannot serve the parents, and if the parents do not become one, heaven and earth cannot become one.  
The fall occurred when one brother led the other into the path of death while claiming to go the way of life. However, from an absolute perspective, both brothers had issues.  
Now we must be Abel-like beings who can move Cain to repentance. I must become someone who can manage the left and right through this wise struggle. I must also be a brother whom the parents can boast about. Only when I can show my brother in place of him can I start on the brother's path. I must move centered on myself in a spherical manner. Standing on this standard is standing on the original standard.  
We must be able to move above and below, front and back, left and right to move heaven and earth.  
The Lord who is coming is the True Brother who says He will bear the suffering of the younger brother. He comes with the position of the heavenly Cain, taking on the younger brother's difficulties and pains as His own while saying that the blessings will be for the younger brother. He comes with the heart of a husband and the heart of a parent, coming on behalf of God. He is the Messiah, so everything must be discussed with Him. Only then can we become beings that are not invaded by Satan. All of you gathered here must become such beings and must not fall short.

13)  
To Possess the Land of Blessing  
<Summary of the Message> For members who have been here for more than three years, there will be great trials. If left alone, they will become people unrelated to the teacher.  
We are currently living in the wilderness era. However, just because the wilderness era ends does not mean everything is over. When the wilderness era ends, we must fight with all our strength for the restoration of Canaan. We are living in the 40-year wilderness period for the global restoration of Canaan. This world is God's world, the world of all humanity, and we live looking forward to the day when we can say it is my world. This work cannot be entrusted to the hands of leaders; it must be done by our hands. To do this, one cannot be someone who cannot manage themselves on the wilderness journey. The death that the Israelite nation suffered in the wilderness was due to being pushed out of an environment where they could be blessed as a nation.  
We must long for the land of blessing, Canaan. Even Jacob, when he died, asked to be buried in his hometown. Otherwise, he would not be Israel. The Israelite nation received the distribution of the land of blessing without realizing it. We too must struggle until we receive blessings. The current time requires a certain conviction and determination.  
October 21, 1962 (Sunday), 2 PM, Former Headquarters Church.
* This message has been organized and published from the 22nd issue of <Seonghwa> (December 1, 1962).

70   To Possess the Blessed Land
Those who fear the wilderness era will perish. To step on the blessed land, one must have a global ideology. The history of Israel is about fighting for the sovereignty of individuals, families, nations, and the world. Has the first Israel and the second Israel, Christianity, completely established a foundation for individuals, families, nations, and states? They have not. Therefore, a decisive operation must be performed, which is the great judgment.

Today, 3 billion people live in the world of Satan. The history of humanity is all about bridging everyone to one person. That person is Jesus. He had no chosen individuals, families, tribes, nations, or the world. Therefore, He had to establish victorious individuals, families, societies, nations, and the world in His time. That was Jesus' mission.

Originally, the Israelite people should have passed one person at a time to the heavenly side during the 400 years of suffering in Egypt. If Joseph had many supporters when he became the Prime Minister at the age of 30, there would have been no need for suffering. However, Joseph could not fulfill that mission and died. Likewise, Jesus was supposed to lay the foundation as a Prime Minister-level figure in heavenly affairs but also died without fulfilling His mission.

Until now, Christianity has fought on behalf of the oppressed in Egypt. In the meantime, they have been waiting for a leader. This is the messianic thought of Christianity. The one who comes to take on the responsibility of resolving this is the Messiah. Unbeknownst to them, the Messiah comes with the mission of Moses, who worked in the palace for 40 years, and the mission of Christ.

So, what will the Messiah do when He comes to this earth? He will live, but not for individuals; He will live with God, with the heavenly saints, and with the land of hope. He will live in this world of Satan. However, because Jesus came to this earth and could not fulfill that mission, He is spiritually carrying out this work today.

Now we must carry out this mission on a national level through individuals, families, and nations. We must enter Canaan as the 12 tribes. Thus, we must make the seven nations of Canaan tremble. If that happens, there will be no need for fighting.

71 
Next, we must move them from the position of the enemy's slaves to the position of God's servants. This was the mission that the Israelite people had during the time of Moses and Jesus. However, they did not do it properly. Because of that sin, 6 million Israelites died. Now, if we make another mistake, 60 million will die.

It is not God's will for only the second generation to enter Canaan from the wilderness. If that were the case, the elders would have been exhausted and all died. The chosen Israelite people must not only offer worship or sacrifices. Just as God works with a universal ideology, they must advance with a universal ideology. Today, if the second Israel, Christianity, lives denominationally without such an ideology, it will perish.

How should the remaining nations proceed in the future? They must not live with habitual ideologies or the customary ideologies of the Old Testament. A new revolution is necessary. They must struggle nationally, centered on God's ideology, within the world of Satan. They must fight by entering the enemy's country. Even in luxurious places like the palace, they must think in their hearts, "These people..." No matter how well they eat and live luxuriously, they must be people of heaven, not of that world.

The struggle begins with individuals. Naturally, a struggle of heart and body unfolds. One must win in this fight to be called by God. Moses was called as a national leader because his heart for the nation was stronger than his desire for a luxurious position.

God raised Moses and brought him into the highest place of glory, and then He brought him into the lowest place. In doing so, He disregarded the glory of the world of Satan. Jesus did the same.

Satan tempted Jesus, saying, "Turn these stones into bread, jump from the top of the temple, and I will give you all the kingdoms of the world if you worship me," but Jesus did not respond to this.

One must think of the heavenly people who are in a pitiful position even in the highest place of the world of Satan. In that sense, Moses killing the Egyptians was a good deed. It is undoubtedly a sin, but emotionally, it cannot be accused. That is why he could be raised as a national leader. The same goes for Jacob and Jesus. They did not care about the glory of the world or death. Such people have come forth with a historical mission.

Therefore, in personal struggles, one must be able to let go of personal glory or family happiness. That is the standard for public life. Jesus lived such a life for 30 years in personal struggles. If the Israelite people had followed Jesus, the issues of individuals, families, nations, and even the world would not have been a problem. However, that did not happen.

Those who will enter heaven must have the confidence to participate in the struggles of families, individuals, nations, and the world. Even if their children fall, even if their nation is abandoned, even if the world is abandoned, they must step over it. Even if it is a glorious position or a beloved wife, if it goes against the will, they must let go without hesitation. This is not something the teacher made up. It is the principle of restoration.

Even if one dies, they must leave something behind for this will. They should want to drop even a single hair close to the temple. Did the Israelite people do that? The heart must precede that this will cannot be exchanged for anything. If exchanged, one becomes an enemy. How many people are there with such a sense of responsibility?

You must participate in the struggles of individuals, families, nations, and the world. Those who say they cannot go because it is difficult should go. Such people defile tradition.

If you do not go, you will perish. You must be pushed. If you say to go even into a furnace, you must go. The Israelite people had to go as far as Moses went. The blessings are not given so that they can live well. They are given to expand the foundation of the will. We, the saints of the end times, must fulfill all the substantial responsibilities.

If the whole cannot cross at once, we must bridge one by one to cross. Those in the wilderness era cannot discuss the respect for their personality or face. They must say that it does not matter if they wear ragged clothes. The Israelite people had to follow Moses, whether they liked it or not. That is a decisive fact. There is no objection. If there is an objection, one must die. Even if it becomes a disgrace, they must go.

73 
That is the path to happiness. 

If Korea sits idly by, thinking it is blessed, will everything be fine? If we cannot take responsibility, that blessing will go abroad.

Is the path of restoration for the teacher to walk? It is for you to walk. From now on, even if someone falls beside you, you must leave them behind. You must be resolute.

You must have such conviction that even if the world offers you any position or glory, you can reject it. You must live a life that cannot be exchanged even for the whole world. You must live an ideological life centered on God. Moses and Jesus became historical figures because they had extraordinary thoughts. Should we leave corpses in the world of Satan while searching for the world of heavenly sovereignty?

In public standards, private standards do not apply. You cannot do whatever you want and sleep as much as you want.

That is why the Unification Church is moving based on the wilderness era. In the past, there were no houses. Now, if you go to the countryside and get a room, you can put up a sign and hold worship. However, in the beginning, we were pushed around and covered in filth. We could not do our national responsibilities, so we could not. Even my sleeping under a blanket is for you. Even now, I want to go out to the fields and sleep on the stones.

Will you be led by the ceiling? Will you be led by emotions? You must have a heart of public indignation. The teacher also goes out with a sword in one heart. You must not be careless. Even the blessed will be pushed out. Those who do not go will perish.

If you cannot take responsibility, you will be accused. 

In the future, do not let your children step on graves. 

What will happen if Korea cannot take responsibility? Look at what happened to the Jewish people when they could not take responsibility. That mission passed to the Gentiles. Those who blurred the path of Moses and divided the nation are enemies. Just wait and see who perishes. The teacher does not deal with personal enemies. He deals with global enemies. He says to go and see.

To restore the world, we must make the environment smooth, and that is how we proceed. Do you want to go or not? If you want to go, you must pray with your heart.

To enter heaven, one must become a person who can say no to the glory of this world and even to treasures that cannot be found again in the world.

In conclusion, a global ideology that can dominate the future world must emerge. If you accept such an ideology, family issues will not be a problem. Wealth and everything that everyone considers good will not be a problem. Even if placed in a position of glory, it will not be a problem. Such a global ideology must emerge. If a nation has citizens who can abandon their families, it will quickly be rebuilt.

Our ideology is an ideology that has been confined to families and nations. Therefore, we must first revolutionize from the family. One must be able to abandon their wife and children if they go against the will. Such a principle is the principle of the restoration era, and such a nation is the nation of the restoration era. When such a principle emerges, such a nation will also emerge.

I am a chosen people for heaven and earth, so I need nothing. My only desire is to throw the bomb of truth for the world. If there is no conviction and shock in that, it is better to go your own way. Such a person has no relationship with God. Conversely, if one has such determination, shock, and conviction, they must die here even if it means death.

If it is not worthy before the will, 

You must say, "What does it matter to you and me?" 

Only then can you go to the ideal world and ideological world governed by God. Even if you die on this path, you must be willing to die with this ideology and this leader. Otherwise, you will part ways anyway. Parting is just a matter of time.

Until this will is established globally, you must not lose that heart. Therefore, we must work quickly. If we give up halfway while building God's castle, who will come to build it? In the end, someone else will build that castle. Then we will be nothing but servants. The master does not stop.

We must think that living together in the heavenly world while abandoning the glory of the world of Satan is blessed. If you understand the will, a mother with children will not be able to sleep at night. You must know the time. When the time comes, you will find that it has already passed. We must stay up all night praying and serving others.

After October, each person must make a one-on-one promise. Do you think it will be easy to go to heaven? God has been nurturing one Adam for 6,000 years. We must cut off the branches of the wild olive tree and graft in the true olive tree in its place.

The Correct Attitude of Heavenly People
The attitude of heavenly people is to abandon all the highest glories of the world of Satan and be willing to go to the lowest place in the heavenly world, even the place of death. Before worrying about their own livelihood, they must worry about the livelihood of the church. You may be working hard with your blood, but in fact, you must become a faithful servant of heaven by offering not only your blood but also your body.

Now is the time to rise for the world. The period from October of this year to April of next year will be a crucial time.

In the coming years, our Unification Church members must spread more than the Americans who are spread all over the world, and we must show a lifestyle that is better than what Americans demonstrate. The number of world travelers must also exceed theirs. And we must become the best in the labor market. We must be stronger than the communists.

The Unification Church must produce many global missionaries. We must create an environment where they can be accepted worldwide without any procedures. They are the saviors of their countries. To do this, we must endure a lot of global hardships. *

14)
Work hard with faith, love, and wisdom
<Summary of the Message> Those who leave words between blessed couples are enemies of the heart. Children born in such a state of disunity will forever be treated as Cain.

Those who cannot unite cannot enter through the door of blessing. God establishes and repays those who have received blessings but have gone astray. In other words, it is about setting absolute standards of words, heart, and character and judging accordingly.

In the future, if you make mistakes, the angels will accuse you. And the ancestors of the past will accuse you. This is to make you suffer to avoid this.

Before hard work and suffering, even angels and Satan bow their heads. Who can accuse someone who is willing to die for the will and shed tears for the will? Therefore, you must become a person who is pitied for being unfortunate while holding onto the will.

Until now, the teacher has not been able to rest for even 10 minutes. If you establish loyalty in places where no one can go, everyone will eventually submit.

God allows individuals to undergo trials with the cross attached to establish families. In this way, He leads them through trials step by step. If you suffer at the time you should receive glory, you will not be accused. There must be occurrences that move the father to tears. Tears must not cease from the altars across the nation.

October 27, 1962 (Saturday), at the former headquarters church.
* This message was given during a national regional leaders' meeting and has been organized from notes taken by former association president Yoo Yu-won. The title was added by the editor.

77 
What the teacher has prayed for over six years is faith, love, and wisdom. Faith is the belief in what even God cannot believe, love is the love that everyone rejoices in, and wisdom is the wisdom that is not the wisdom of Solomon.

It is to create people who can abandon their families for the sake of the nation. The term "suffering" means to be revived through hardship. *

15)
The Fruits of Humanity
<Summary of the Message> The Day of Children carries a providential significance. There have been many miserable days that we cannot forget—such as the day Adam fell and the day Noah made mistakes—but there has been no day that God truly rejoiced. We must not meet today without the resolve to erase all these sad days.

Today is the day of harvest and the day of children. If seeds are sown in spring, they can be harvested in autumn, but God has not had a day of harvest. He has also not had a day to sow what has been harvested.

What is harvested by the hands of parents must be sown and reaped through the hands of beloved children. Humanity has gone through the history of sowing and reaping seeds.

When God created Adam, He intended to sow seeds, but they were broken off while growing. God has longed for a day when He can sow again, and this day is the day of judgment.

Among humanity, we have been looking forward to a day of hope when two fruits must be harvested; this day is the day of the Second Coming. The day of the Lamb's feast is the day of creating true couples as they originally are, and this is the day of judgment at the end. Therefore, the title of the message I will deliver today is 

The Fruits of Humanity.

Among those gathered here, there may be some who have something to boast about in various ways. There may be those who have something to boast about in the Lord or in their families, but that is not what... 

October 28, 1962 (Sunday), at the former headquarters church.
* This statement was made during the Children's Day event on the 1st of October in the lunar calendar, and it has been organized and published based on what former Association President Yoo Hyowon recorded in his notebook.
79
It did not start with God's joy and blessing. This is all false, and thus it cannot shed the mask of corruption. This world is a field of tares. How much of the tare's element is in my body! I must discard this and put in something better. The bloodline flows with the blood of murderers. I am the source of all sin. What sins could our ancestors have not committed! The question is whether I can stand in the position of good soil or not. The Way (道) begins from negation. After negating the heart, the highest religion is the one that negates the heart. The Way people sometimes have to stand in the position of captives. While eating a single rice ball, one must think about how to escape from this fallen world. The day when the barbed wire is cut is the day of the great judgment. One must cut the barbed wire to go where one wants to go. Therefore, the barbed wire of the individual, family, society, nation, and world must be cut. The main focus should be on the heart, religion should be heart-centered, and philosophy should be heart philosophy. Whether 6,000 years ago or now, the heart remains the same. The statement that Jesus is the only begotten Son means that no one else is a son. The term Savior means that there is no one else but Him. He also said, "I am the bridegroom, and you are the bride." When we combine these words, Jesus must be the owner of a large family. The statement that one life is more precious than the world is a statement centered on the heart, and it refers to Jesus Himself. Politics must also be heart-centered politics. The ideology of national sovereignty and any ideology in the world must be like that. When God comes to this earth, if there is even one person who can drink water without food and still make God happy, this land will not perish. There is no room on this earth for God to set foot. Teaching people to feel that such a God is pitiful is religion. Let us liberate God. Since God is sad, the Way people should not be happy. Therefore, the Way people must suffer. If it is a religion of the heart, it must be able to teach that God is pitiful. To liberate history, one must become the one who can resolve God's historical heart. When Jesus said, "Love me more," it was a statement for eternity. It is until the grafting is done. I may be insignificant, but the words are great. Can I ask God, who is more pitiful and suffering than I am, to suffer more? God will come where there is such a heart. Only those who seek to meet the Father who is weeping on the cross can meet Him. One must become a filial child in a sad and miserable place. One must be prepared to go to any country with the determination to do so. One must gather money with tears of blood. For those who have formed a couple, the next seven months are a special period. The inheritance from Jesus is received at Golgotha. It is also an inheritance that is given after establishing the one who will inherit it. The one who receives this inheritance is the historical heir. During these seven months, one must receive the inheritance from Jesus. To do this, one must evangelize more than three people. This period is one that will not come again. One must be devoted to evangelism day and night. If one fails to take responsibility during this period, it will be extended until the fourth lunar month. *
16)
In Search of the Path of Life
<Summary of the Words> Whether you like it or not, you were born from your parents. Upon being born, you must have realized that there is heaven and earth and that humanity exists. You must also have realized that there are various societies, nations, and territories in this world. Seeing this, you would want to break through the complex boundaries of this world and create a world where everyone can care for each other, meet, and rejoice together. 
The Reality of Human Life
Such a desire exists in everyone, but what is the reality? People doubt, envy, and are jealous of each other, and they cannot unite as they wish. Yet everyone is looking for someone they can meet without doubt, someone they can meet without fear, and someone they can meet with only joy. However, have we ever been a truly necessary person, one who cannot be absent at any time, someone whom others want to see over and over again, someone whose life cannot be exchanged for anything else, someone they want to showcase to the universe? Of course, within the family, we may have temporarily become someone necessary for our parents and siblings or within the small circle of life, but that is limited to a confined scope. 
On November 1, 1962 (Thursday), at the former headquarters church.
* This statement was made during the opening ceremony of the 14th National Evangelist Training Session and has been organized and published from <Seonghwa> No. 21 (dated November 1, 1962).
82 In Search of the Path of Life
Even your parents, after bringing you into this world, become anxious and uneasy in fear. This is because the world is worrisome and untrustworthy, a world of fear, and at the same time, it is a world from which one cannot escape due to some unknown entanglement. Moreover, it is a world swept by the waves of death. So why has this world become like this? Because of the fall. The consequence of the fall is death. The history of humanity has been a history of seeking life, that is, the path of life from this death. This path cannot be paved by humans alone, so something must be added to it. 
Human ancestors had at least a little history of not falling, but we do not even have that. In this regard, our ancestors had a better heart and a better standard of heart to serve God than we do, yet they fell, so how can we be saved by our own strength? Therefore, something must be added to human strength. 
To find the true path of life for the individual, one must find the path that allows the family to live. Then the individual will simply pass. To find the true path of life for the family, one must find the path that allows the tribe to live. Then the family will simply pass. For the nation to find the true path of life, the state must find the path that allows the nation to live. Then the nation will simply pass. For the state to find the true path of life, the world must find the path that allows the state to live. Then the state will simply pass. Thus, there must be something that leads one step ahead of what the times demand. 
There is certainly a force of some existence at work there; who could that existence be? If the owner of that power is the worst being, then there can be no ideal terms such as salvation, happiness, or peace in the human world. However, if the best being is the owner of that power, then only hopeful terms can remain in this world. 
Looking at myself, I have both good and evil hearts within me, and looking at society, there are two currents of good and evil that are always in conflict. 
Where is the place of death, and where is the place of life? 
To live means to discard the elements of evil and graft onto the essence of good, while to die means to discard the elements of good and graft onto the essence of evil. Therefore, a good person is one who fights against evil in their life, while an evil person is one who fights against good. A sage is one who introduces measures and paths to win against evil in order to save the world of evil. 
God Who Has Saved Humanity
We are seeking good. However, since we cannot find this good with our own strength alone, we must combine the strength of something. Therefore, we are looking for the protagonist of good power. If there is one who can strike down the beast of Satan before the good God and grant the authority of victory to us humans, then that person is the protagonist we are seeking, the Messiah, the highest victor representing God. 
If this person destroys evil and creates individuals, families, societies, nations, worlds, and the universe centered on the Creator God, that is the ideal world, the kingdom of heaven on earth. That place is where God hopes to be, where humanity hopes to be, and where the original mind of humanity seeks to go. However, in this world, there are paths leading towards that way and paths leading in the opposite direction. These two sides must collide and be resolved into one, and the one who brings the ideology to handle these two sides is the Messiah. 
We may pride ourselves on having a living conscience and a living body, but we are dead because we have become captives of Satan, unable to live within the connections of good. Therefore, we must break out of the bars that surround us. Moreover, there are two masters in our hearts and around us, making peace impossible and causing continuous suffering. What resolution and determination must we have as we seek the path of life? The bars that surround us are none other than this body, so we must mobilize our conscience to break through these bars. That time will be the end. 
To humans who do not even realize they are trapped, God has established religion internally to allow them to live according to their conscience and has provided teachings of good externally to guide them. Although we live in a world of death, He has raised up saints and righteous people who can live in a new world, a world of peace, that is not of this generation. 
84 In Search of the Path of Life
At first, God established a servant to work with Him, and then He sent a child who is one with God to shock people's consciences and carry out the work of connecting internally and externally. In other words, He has worked to have people mobilize their inner conscience to strike down the bars, that is, their bodies, and instead graft the body of a child who is one with God in its place. 
The path of the Way is a path that begins with the negation of the body. Therefore, one must negate the individual body, negate the family body, and even negate the social body. For this reason, God has established the ideology of good and has called upon humanity to cut off all bars, that is, bodies, and to come forth victorious. 
Dear ones! As you know, the Unification Church is not a social organization but a religious organization. It is a group that serves God. Therefore, there must be an ideology here, and this ideology must be something high and great that expands the foundation of the highest conscience of humanity, paving a victorious stage of life that can eternally serve God and can overcome and surpass everything in the world. 
A teaching (religion) that expands the foundation of human conscience and allows people to serve God with sincerity is what opens the path of life for humanity. This ideology, which is more precious than anything in this world, must emerge to create people who can discard their bodies and carry an absolute self. 
The Purpose of Training
We must walk this tremendous path, but how should we walk it? The things that are extremely good can only be understood in comparison to what is opposite to them. 
From the fall until today, there should not have been a history. Our goal is to return to the state of Adam before the fall. That Adam knew only God and had no fear, so we too must return to a place where we serve only God and know no fear. Thus, we must understand the sorrow of having lost God and be able to compare the me who knows no fear with the me who was in fear. 
Furthermore, we must know who led us to the fall. Did Adam fall alone? Did God create him that way? Did it happen inevitably? It was because of the devil. It is because of the chief of evil, the devil. We must have the conviction to find the being who instilled fear in us, who built walls of fear around us, who pushed us into the place of death, who made us lose God, and who violated and exploited us, and to gather all our grievances, pain, and sorrow into one arrow and pierce it into the heart of that enemy, the devil. 
Because the enemy remains and the process of fighting remains, God has not rested for a single day and has fought until now. Therefore, we must also have the heart of public indignation and resolve to fight against the enemy, even if we lose everything. The one who has paved and opened this path has done so, so I must also resolve to walk that path and put it into practice. If I do not do so, I will be unrelated to the center. 
To cut ties with the enemy and be liberated from the enemy, we are receiving training to cultivate a heart of public indignation towards the enemy and to become victorious. 
The Unification Church is a place that teaches how to fight and win against Satan. Therefore, you must resolve to become warriors of victory and engage in training to cultivate your heart and character through the words. To do this, you must negate your body. The inner person is not affected by external conditions such as hunger and cold, so you must learn how to completely negate the outer person, placing your conscience in the highest positive position and becoming a victor. *
17)
Leave Behind Many Hard-earned Materials
<Summary of the Words> What is seen moving in Korea is also moving in Japan based on that. Thus, the movement of the headquarters has significant meaning. 
A wife must make her husband loyal by suffering while carrying a baby. Even if she has to leave the baby, she must evangelize centered on the Trinity. 
One must establish a way to practice what the teacher has said. If one cannot go out to evangelize, then at least they should pray anxiously. The teacher does not intend to create a privileged class. To become a privileged class, one must suffer. 
When foreigners come, they may criticize you. When the teacher goes abroad, you must be the ones he can boast about by name. 
Each family should hold meetings to select three representative people to help each other and build up together. The mistakes of family members greatly hinder the development of the church. 
Children must feel the emotions of hardworking parents. They must have conditions to boast about their parents when they grow up. 
Hyowon must practice what the teacher has decided. Mothers of babies must also be mobilized. If they do not show loyalty, good sons and daughters will not be born. 
Do not think that the teacher will always be with you. You must be able to do it even without the teacher. You must prepare and train based on the standard that the teacher is not present. 
Do not try to rely on the teacher's cooperation. That is how it becomes filial (孝) and loyal (忠). 
Tithing is something everyone must do. One must be prepared to give tithes up to the three principles for heaven, the nation, and the world. That is the principle. 
If the world can weep because the teacher is in chains, is that not also good? The teacher's suffering is good in this sense. 
Who will the teacher take with him in the future? It will be those who have suffered. Therefore, you must have many hard-earned materials. This is creating the history of your family and the history of your tribe. 
In loving a baby, one must place even more importance on the purpose. Everything is precious because of that one purpose! 
This applies to mothers as well, but do not engage in one-on-one love. Establish a foundation of heart and love. 
The higher the love is compared to one's own love, the more stimulation it brings. If there is no heart for the purpose, one will even dislike the other person passing by. 
If a husband is lying down and sleeping, I want to encourage you to be a wife who can say, "Why are you sleeping so much?" and wake him up. 
Have you reached a position where you can boast about having a baby? Just as you love your child, think about whether God can love you in the same way. 
The Father gave His beloved Son to the cross. If a brother dies fighting for the purpose, do you have the heart to feel indignant? To feel such emotions, one must suffer. 
If something happens to family members, it is reflected in the teacher. If you feel that it is reflected in you, you must be moved to think that heaven teaches even someone like me to be concerned. You must understand the work the teacher is doing.
You must take responsibility for what Koreans cannot. Families must suffer, and the nation must suffer. Since we have not properly received the gifts given, those who know this must fill the empty valleys. We must first roll stones into that valley.

The teacher sometimes appears foolish and ignorant. The teacher wants to select a few families and make them suffer greatly to see how the descendants turn out...

God wants to distribute blessings. You must prepare to be a vessel that can receive those blessings. When the Unification Church gives blessings, it gives them along with the blessings of the world. Therefore, you should not think of this blessing as solely your own. God also gave Israel a global blessing, but they perished because they thought it was only for themselves.

What kind of lineage and connection will the teacher's family establish? They will connect with families that are even more loyal than the teacher's family. When the teacher accepts a daughter-in-law or son-in-law, it must be from a family that heaven and earth do not accuse.

Every part of the body—mouth, eyes, nose, ears, and limbs—must suffer. If we do not fight like soldiers on the battlefield, we cannot overcome this hill.

**Practice and Restoration**
<Summary of the Words> Before creating all things, God is the thinking Father and the acting Father. The being that God has established in His place is Adam and Eve. God desires that humans think of Him as their Father, think of all things, think of what He has done, and then think of themselves. Not knowing this will of God is the fall.

To make Adam capable of experiencing God's heart of creation, God left one area of responsibility for Adam to pass through.

No matter what work you do centered on yourself, it cannot be established before God. The purpose of God's restoration work is to create people who know and practice the God who thinks and acts first.

The reason for establishing and enabling me to practice and act is that we have a shared responsibility. Finding and establishing this mental foundation is the restoration work. Therefore, all our thoughts must be directed toward the realization of the Father’s ideal of creation.

We must stand in the position of a second God in family life and social life. We must seek ourselves with the heart of God who created heaven and earth and must practice according to the purpose of creation. If we fail to do this, just as God told Adam and Eve not to eat, you will find yourselves in a similar position.

November 27, 1962 (Tuesday, Lunar Calendar November 1) Morning Worship, at the Headquarters Church.

* This message has been organized from notes taken by former Association President Yoo Woo-yeon, and the title was added by the editor.

We must all become people who think and act like God. God created in darkness. He did not create in a good place, but in a place that was not good. Therefore, we must also start from difficult places. The more difficult it is, the more God longs for people. Thus, we must start from the lowest position.

To conceive life, there must be morning sickness. Just as God labored to create heaven and earth, one must go through internal and external pain for life to be born.

The principle must be to carry God’s heart and lineage. Such things are not recorded anywhere in the Bible. The reason the spiritual world has been in a holding pattern until now is that there has been no one on this earth with such a heart. 

To serve heaven, we must have a personality that does not shy away from anything. To become such a person, one must have the determination to fight for heaven. One must be filled with the conviction to fight and win against the enemy on the battlefield of sorrow. Even when clashing with the enemy there, not yielding, not being defeated, and not breaking is the standard of personality. Only those with such a personality can become the sons and daughters of heaven. Without such a person, one cannot become the son or daughter of heaven. There are no conditions for slander against such a person. 

One must become a person who cannot yield when it comes to what Jesus desired. A personality that cannot be exchanged for the world is needed. The complexity of history is to align with the path the teacher is taking. The period until April is crucial. We must fulfill the responsibilities and missions entrusted to us. 

Until now, we have shed tears to resolve grievances, but from now on, we must shed tears for victorious sovereignty. We must shed tears not for the grievances of our ancestors but for the world and the people. Only with such a heart can we fulfill our mission. 

The establishment of Elder Song was due to the patriotic spirit for thirty million people, faithfully serving without knowing the future. Such things must expand. We must carry such a heart. We must be ignited with righteous indignation. From now on, if we raise a resentful heart, we cannot forgive. 

There are no people shedding tears for that country. Now, it has become a world of substantial hope. We must have a heart greater than that of an exiled king. Now is the age of offense. The grieving multitude is only you. Who in this country will become that? 

Start from the Lowest Place 

God blessed Adam, but Adam could not possess it. Whether one possesses it or not depends on oneself. Just as Satan attacked while slandering, we must also attack while slandering. To do that, we must first be hit and first endure. After sending the flesh toward the path of Golgotha, we must establish the reality on behalf of the spiritual world. 

You may have a secondary three-year period. We must also move forward for the world. 

To truly subdue all people, we must start from the lowest place. Now, we do not know what commands the teacher will give. You will not know how much internal pain there has been until I bless you. I have established you with the heart of drawing the last card from the gambling table. 

The earth may seem worthless, but it has the elements that can absorb everything. The people of this age have caused the teacher more suffering than anyone else, so they must think with gratitude as time goes on. The teacher explodes at the slightest touch of someone’s true heart. 

136   God’s Will and the Responsible Person 

However, until now, no one has been able to touch it. 

I have entered every valley of God’s heart. We must not forget that God has come with indescribable sorrow. We must move forward with the heart that God has come with. 

I hope to fight with a complete body and achieve complete victory. Because the heart and lineage are different, a personality that can unify that heart and lineage is needed. Even if one has not been filial to their parents, if they bear children and raise them while sincerely repenting, the path of atonement will open.
