32) We Are the Reality of Hope with Responsibility 

<Summary of the Message> We must go out to evangelize in more than seven countries in the future. You must become the central ancestors of Korea and the reality of restoration. 

Due to the fall of human ancestors, you have become the ancestors in reverse. You must become the ancestors of the first and second Israel. The children born from now on will become the third Israel. 

The Unification Church members in Korea now are not beings that remain as individuals. They must be connected to the spiritual world and future generations. Therefore, I must think about how to establish global connections. 

We must be set apart as offerings. If the offerings become dirty, they will be slandered forever. Therefore, we must carry a heartistic connection. 

We are the reality of hope for the past, present, and future. That is why we can connect the hopes of the past, present, and future centered on us. 

We are the reality of hope with responsibility. If we do not establish a standard here, it cannot be done. Thus, we must move beyond the standard established centered on the teacher. We must also engage in external struggles centered on the teacher. Wherever we go, it is to save the four directions of east, west, south, and north. Therefore, we must go with the Father. The history until now has been made without knowing this fact. 

January 30, 1963 (Wednesday, lunar January 6), 2:10 AM, former headquarters church. 
* These words were spoken during the 43rd anniversary celebration of the teacher’s birth, compiled from notes taken by former association president Yoo Hyowon. The title was added by the editor. 

138   We Are the Reality of Hope with Responsibility 

We have laid the foundation in the three-year period. From now on, we must take the offensive no matter what happens. 

We must make many people joyful with our sorrow. We must do so until we are completely offerings. From the moment we become completely offerings, we become sacred objects. This gathering is a meeting to offer such offerings. 

Now, after we have become one and completely offerings, if we curse, it will be as we curse. 

We are not resurrected spiritual beings but beings that encompass both spirit and flesh. If we make a mistake here, we can strike it and establish it as a secondary offering. 

By giving up one person, we can also save a nation. The most straightforward path as offerings is the path of hardship. The world must be saved with heart. Therefore, we must endure hardships. What would have happened if Ms. Bongchun had not gone to Japan three years ago?
If we cannot go out to evangelize in seven countries this year, we must select seven locations within the United States and send people there. 
When one base goes, the other two bases must prepare everything for him. 
Pray for this. 
Each department head of the association should divide the Seoul district and assign other districts to the members. 
We must go not with money but with faith. We must go out strong and courageous, with faith, will, and heart, just like Joshua and Caleb. 
Since Adam could not offer a sacrifice to God, Cain and Abel offered it instead. Therefore, the children must go through hardship. Only then can they understand God's heart. The second three-year period is a time of familial suffering. 
What you currently possess is not yours. 
A person who cannot feel pity when seeing the shape achieved through the suffering of others must walk a path greater than the suffering of that person. 
The main sanctuary that must be built with the sincerity of Korean members 
<Summary of the message> We must build the headquarters church. Those who think it would be good to build a church with their own money are construction preparation committee members. The headquarters church must be built only by the hands of Korean people. 
We had to create 70,000 members over three years. 
The Father is in a position to give, so He cannot ask fallen humans for anything. Therefore, humans must do it themselves. 
The reason the Father could not teach the secret of the fall was for this reason. Because it is a principle, He could not announce it. Therefore, humans must find that secret and negotiate with God. 
In the future, bridges must be built, and to build bridges, there must be people who go under the bridge and into the water. There must also be cement, gravel, and sand. 
When the line is trodden, the wall set by Satan collapses. 
Who will govern this country in the future? 
If something has value, treating it below that value becomes evil. 
From a providential perspective, we are like those on top of a hill. Therefore, we must settle the past and move forward. Only then can Satan not accuse us. God is at the headquarters church on January 31, 1963 (Thursday) at 11 AM.

The main sanctuary that must be built with the sincerity of Korean members 
God wants to untangle the things entangled in sin, but if they have no desire to be untangled, the responsibility will return to them. 
We must not build the sanctuary with money that is shameful to our conscience. What should we do when we have to receive money that we cannot dare to accept? You are the descendants of Adam and Eve, and you are the descendants of the sinners who killed Jesus.... Burn with public indignation

Attitude toward training

The first three days will be difficult to get through.

February 5, 1963 (Tuesday) at 7:30 PM, at the former headquarters church. 
* This message was a speech of encouragement given at the opening ceremony of the 15th National Evangelist Training Conference, compiled from the content published in <Seonghwa> No. 24 (March 1, 1963). 
Burn with public indignation 
Sometimes, a person like a grandson may inevitably speak informally to someone like a grandfather. Even so, you must endure and move forward. You must have a public heart that lives for the whole, forgetting yourself. When giving advice, the one giving it should do so on behalf of the father, and the one receiving it should accept it as if the father is giving it. 
You must always live centered on public standards. Until now, there has been no public standard in this vast universe. There has been nothing that can be recognized by the past, present, and even the future, something that can be recognized by the three ages. When the highest public standard appears, the universe will be filled. Public means that everything is included. Everything about individuals, families, and nations must be public. Those who cannot find public standards cannot find themselves. Humans must be absorbed before public standards. 
After overcoming the initial six days, you will begin to taste the training around the seventh day. Then, after two weeks and around the third week, that is, after about 20 days, you will finally get on the right track. 
Now, I ask you to become one and go through this 40-day period well. Especially now, there is no water. When a person is hungry and there is no water, they will face immediate difficulties. How grateful would we be if there were water when we are extremely thirsty and hungry? If there is water, we can feel gratitude even in hunger. Furthermore, when there is neither food nor water, try breathing air. Then you will understand how delicious that air is. It would be good if we could barely survive with a little food, a little water, and a little air, and thus create people who can feel gratitude. The same goes for sunlight. 
The most precious things are always treated as cheap. Those who think the most precious things are worthless are evil people. If the sun, air, water, and rice go on strike, people will die helplessly. Therefore, training is necessary to feel the value of these things. 
From now on, I would like to say a few words to you. Everyone has the same body and features. However, in terms of the content that the body possesses, there are countless variations. Then, among the countless humans with such diverse contents, where should I place my standard? None of our ancestors after Adam and Eve can be a standard. If we take a moment to step away from all our relationships in this complicated world and quietly reflect on ourselves, we will realize that nations and people are not absolute beings but relative beings. Therefore, hands, eyes, noses, mouths, arms, and legs all move for relative purposes. When these come together for a single purpose, they require some relative object. When they move like this, there will be something good or bad. 
The path of religion 
Where does the nation itself originate from in this universe? Humans do not know this origin. Did I come from an unknown existence? 
Then why did I come? There must be some purpose for which I came. However, it is not enough just to become a subject or an object of a counterpart. There must be conditional content needed here; what is that? This is a significant issue. What is necessary for me to exist today? Around me, there are front, back, left, right, and above and below. 
Then, what is the motive and subject that made me exist among those around me? That is God. This is what has been called God, Kami-sama, etc. 
The purpose perspective until now has not only been human-centered but also based on the relationship between God and humans. Therefore, on one hand, there is God. On the other hand, there are those who claim there is no God. Humans have a present reality centered on themselves and a future purpose that must be achieved. The highest standard that is purpose-oriented based on God is not the body but the heart. If there is something that does not change in a person, what would it be? Conscience. 
If there is a purpose to move forward, even if it means building a bridge, that is God's purpose. That is the will. If we do not establish a will even in a fraction of a second, we cannot enter the world of purpose. When parents hit me, if I know it is for my sake, to make me great, and to give me blessings a thousand or ten thousand times, I will feel gratitude. There is a saying that goes, "Give one more rice cake to the child you hate." This means to quickly bear the fruit of hatred. Conversely, "Hit the beloved child one more time" implies that one should quickly become a reality suitable for hope. 
The reason why all the faith in families and societies is breaking apart today reflects some motivation. Eating what is gained through acts of injustice, such as murder and robbery, becomes a source of self-reproach even after eating. 
Unfortunate reality 
When looking at society today, it is hard to tell what is true. The nouns like mother! and grandmother! are the same, but the contents are all different. Moreover, the reality is that lamentation is surging. A slight mistake can lead to death; this is a global phenomenon today. It is not an exaggeration to say that we have avoided such positions. 
So what should we do? We must cut off everything that hinders us from living truthfully. We must cut off everything that hinders us, even if it is an arm, a head, or a family. We must not be swept away by the main tide of evil, but rather build a bridge and take a different path. Make a decisive choice to go a different way. In the midst of that, moving forward while relying on God is what it means to be religious. To walk a meaningful path in society, one must even abandon their mother and father. Jesus said, "Everyone who has left houses or brothers or sisters or father or mother or children or fields for my sake will receive a hundred times as much and will inherit eternal life." (Matthew 19:29) This was spoken with such a heavenly intention in mind. 
So where will we go? We must choose the path that can bring peace to our hearts. There are strategies for retreating and escaping according to the times, and the path is also like that. There must always be a subject that is beyond humans, that is, a subject greater than myself. Throughout history, there have always been leaders and revolutions. The ideology of religion has emerged from the pursuit of a higher world. To bring about such a revolution, there must be both a leader and an ideology. A reality capable of fulfilling the purpose of heaven and earth is needed. This is the central being based on the messianic thought of a religious leader. Only with such a central being can the existence of God be affirmed. Such a being can be called the center of all humanity. When you meet that being, you will understand the front, back, left, right, and above and below. That being brings the ideals of heaven while also presenting the world of motives and results. 
Is everything that exists today enjoying joy? Has it become a joyful individual, family, society, nation, and world? It has not. However, this world was not created by the motivation of God's creation. For example, suppose there is a couple with a wife who has a deformed arm and a husband with a crooked mouth and is blind, yet they are expecting a baby. Ask that couple about the baby in the womb. They will say it is all good. However, while it is good in the womb, once it is born, it becomes a sad world. Did God create humans with a heart saying, "Oh, how sad"? No. He created with a heart like that when facing delicious food. 
If there had been sadness from the moment of creation, God would not be a father but an enemy. However, God is ultimately a good being. If the motive is good, the process and result must also be good. Yet, while the motive and start of creation are good, the start of human life has been evil. That is why the days of sorrow have continued until now. Humans were created with a sense of universality, so individual sorrow connects to familial, national, and even global sorrow. Personal pain, sorrow, and sin have all become global matters, transcending families, societies, and nations. Therefore, there must be a condition that maximally allows individuals to be joyful so that God can also be joyful. 
Our bodies seek to encounter sorrow, while our hearts seek to encounter joy. The heart opposes the body, and the body opposes the heart. The heart is internal and represents the spirit, while the body is external and represents matter. Just as my heart and body are in opposition, the world is also divided. 
Both idealism and materialism are not completely true. Therefore, anticipating this, God has sent a savior. This is the thought of the savior. God must govern a perfected human to truly be God. That person is one whom the entire world cannot replace, even with any sovereignty. When that person appears, the center of the universe will finally be revealed. The savior is the object of hope and reality. He is the reality that can escape global suffering. By becoming the reality of hope, He can manifest as the reality of victory. 
God has sacrificed many good people. The reality of goodness that He envisioned has become the reality of evil, so to restore it to its original state, God has become the prince of the greatest labor. Goodness prevails, and those who have come out believing in heaven are the religious people. 
The Lord who comes as the subject of theism 
When He comes, we must resemble Him. So where does He come from? He comes from the heart of God. He is the reality beyond God's creation. He is the subject and reality that seeks to invigorate all around. 
Until now, all people have been fake. You are all the fake me. The false me, the storehouse of evil. This must be cleared from the heart. To do this, we must learn. If a hand is not suitable, it must be cut off to live. Do you know what kind of being God is? A dog does not sleep at night for its owner but keeps watch. But has a person done the same? Have you thought about God as much as you value your eyes and ears? We must block all waves of Satan. We must stand in the place where we fall for the sake of goodness. 
All things in the universe we live in are under the dominion of evil. God wishes to establish a world of goodness centered on theism. This is the world of theism centered on God that we must realize today.
I stand before heaven and earth with caution. Such a subject has come alone, and that person is the savior spoken of in Christianity. Understanding this meaning, you must share joys and sorrows with that person. 
Since humans cannot take responsibility on their own, a mediator is needed to bridge the gap. In terms of responsibility, Abraham is the individual type, Jacob is the family type, Moses is the national type, and Jesus is the world type of mediator. This has been passed down in order. Therefore, a religion that connects individuals, families, nations, and the world is a historically significant religion. 
The one who will come in the future will appear as a substantial being representing God with a global mission based on individual, familial, national, and state standards. Moreover, that person will come as the conclusive substance of providence and will also come to fulfill the roles of all the mission bearers who have come and gone throughout history. When a task is accomplished, the grief is resolved to the extent of that accomplishment. Now, the Messiah must come to build the ideal world. 
Every human being is ideal and global. Everyone wants to do well. How much do you want to succeed? How much greed must be satisfied for you to feel content? A servant of God? A son-in-law? That too would likely be unsatisfactory. You would wish to possess God's inheritance and dance while holding onto God's ears. Such is human greed. 
Can a servant do that? Absolutely not. Who can do it? Sons and daughters. Only sons and daughters can be accepted by God. If you possess that noun, there is nothing that does not connect in all matters. If you are in that position, God will also be pleased. This is the hope of humanity. No one can do what God's servants and people can do, but only sons and daughters can do so. Therefore, you must establish true goodness and become an inseparable entity with God, able to call out, "My Father!" 
Only sons and daughters can participate in the glory of victory. That is why God has come to find sons and daughters. The religion that seeks this is Christianity. For this reason, our Unification Church has also emerged centered on Christianity. To be able to say that heaven is good and I am good, one must become a child of God. 
You have come here to become children of God. The purpose of your training is to become children of God in a short time. So, do you just need to go up to the top of God's head and dance? You must also enable God to dance. That is only possible through sons and daughters, who are the embodiment of completed beauty. What God has given as a source of joy to His beloved sons and daughters is all of creation. Therefore, we can say that God's creation of all things was for the sake of sons and daughters. 
Be a son or daughter who brings joy to the Father. 
When our desires and circumstances align with God's, what will God do? He will grant us all things. However, He wishes to have a substantial being who can govern all things and, from that position, give birth to sons and daughters to inherit everything. Such a person will be the one who establishes the front, back, left, right, and up, down as mentioned earlier. 
Everyone is sad if they have no parents, cannot form a couple, and have no children. All of this must be fulfilled, and this is precisely the three great subjects. Centering on this, we must embrace the world. 
I can say, "My Father is my Father. Therefore, the universe created by my Father is mine." The historical hope of the heart is mine, the realistic circumstances are mine, and the future world that He wishes to establish is mine. 
This is what you must be able to say. 
Because the ideology of the bride and groom and the justification of children have been left behind, the King of kings is coming again, and becoming the sons and daughters of this King is the hope of humanity. However, this hope cannot be fulfilled until we connect with God's heart, circumstances, and will. It may work in the human world, but it does not work in the heavenly realm centered on God. That is why we cannot call ourselves sons and daughters, couples, or siblings. Therefore, Jesus said, "Who is my mother and who are my brothers? Those who do the will of my Father..." and also said that the members of your household are enemies. 
To receive the firstborn son who is with the Father, we must welcome the Messiah, who is in the position of the firstborn. That is why people are waiting for him. We must receive him and bless him. Only by receiving blessings can we take our first steps as humans. This is the qualification that can make all things unable to leave us. 
The history of the past has been a history of suffering stained with blood and tears. The Father suffered to give, and the ancestors suffered to receive. Now we must establish a bond with God's heart and fulfill a sovereignty, territory, and people. You are here to find the official laws of humanity: parents, couples, and children. 
The responsibility of the regional leader 
<Summary of the message> The end of April is a crucial period, so efforts must be made for the distribution. 
Each region should have at least 200 members. Regions that are lacking in numbers should combine with nearby regions. Therefore, we must strive. 
As regional leaders, you are not individuals. You must take responsibility for the lives and properties of the community. The members of the region resemble the regional leader. When the regional leader advances, the whole advances, and when the regional leader retreats, the whole retreats. 
The regional leader is connected to heaven and earth through the district leader, association leader, and teacher. An economic crisis will blow into Korea in the future, and all responsibility for this lies with the members. Therefore, we must establish a foundation to guide this nation before it encounters difficulties. 
Even if we are hungry and naked, we must be filled with hope. We must be able to show a prepared content even while starving. 
The regional leader is the leader on the front line. The regional leader must always be prepared to appoint a representative. What could not be achieved in Daegu must be supplemented at the local level. 
When you return, gather the scattered members and reorganize your respective regions. 
February 19, 1963 (Tuesday), 12:45 AM, former headquarters church.

March 1, 1963 (Friday), former headquarters church.

<Summary of the message> Become a single existence. 
Today, I do not know if it is a coincidence that the 3rd graduation ceremony of the Seonghwa Student Association and the 7th graduation ceremony of the expected graduates overlap, but both the 3 and 7 are precious numbers in the history of the restoration providence. 
Always, it is a single person who is the problem. 
If this place you are attending today is blessed, it is an extremely blessed place. Among you, there may be those graduating from school and those who have come from the front lines. However, the content of your lives, whether good or sad, was for a single purpose, and the goal you pursue is also for a single purpose. 
The existence that I am is the one person who can represent the whole. If he can represent the nation, he can dominate the nation, and if he can represent the world, he can dominate the world. If he is a cosmic being, he will be the subject of the cosmos. You now have the responsibility to connect your individual movements to the world and the cosmos. You also have the responsibility to connect the front, back, left, right, and up, down. 
March 15, 1963 (Friday), 7:40 PM, former headquarters church. 
* This message was given during the 3rd graduation ceremony of the Seonghwa Student Association and the 7th graduation ceremony of expected graduates, and it has been organized from the publication in <Seonghwa> No. 25 (April 1, 1963). 
Human beings on the earth live to achieve better relationships and purposes. Even if there are better individuals, families, and social groups, one person is the problem. Among you, the 7th graduates and the 3rd graduates, there is one person who is the problem. In the history of restoration, it has always been a single person who is the problem. During Jacob's time, even among many people, Jacob was the problem. By establishing Jacob, we could finally bless Israel. We cannot deny that all of history until now has been a history seeking a single individual. A single individual, a single family, a single nation, and a single world are what history is woven to find. 
God could not help but bless a family by finding one person, Jacob. This was because He wanted to establish a nation based on that family. In the national era, the one person found and established was Moses. However, did Moses inherit the foundation of Jacob's family as it was? No. After walking for 80 years as a single existence, he finally set out on a 40-year journey as a national existence. Moses was pitiful. Even in the most difficult trials, he established a single personal standard and set out on a 40-year journey as the one national existence. 
The creation ideology that God envisioned in His heart was to love Adam and Eve along with the entire cosmos. God was overflowing with such feelings, but due to the unexpected fall of humanity's ancestors, humans could not inherit the legacy of creation. After going through countless twists and turns, establishing individual expectations, family expectations, and national expectations, He finally sent the Messiah after 4,000 years. 
Throughout history, there have been countless people and countless nations, but no one has established the will of heaven on behalf of heaven. However, Jesus became the one existence who established the will of heaven on behalf of heaven and saved the world. There must be individual representatives, family representatives, national representatives, state representatives, and world representatives. Now is the time to establish vertical representatives horizontally. 
When someone asks you, "Who are you?" you should be able to say, "I am the one existence of the family," or "I am the one existence of the nation." 
No matter how precious God's will or purpose is, if you cannot manifest it, that will or purpose will have nothing to do with you. 
To become a single person, 
Now, when you return, you must act with the spirit and courage of youth, preparing an environment in which you can do so, and also developing your inner character. If I am not properly prepared, who will acknowledge me? If I do not have a proper character, it is a shame before heaven and earth. 
Whether looking at mountains or fields, or observing unfolding events, we can see that now is the time for heaven's will to be fulfilled. In such a time, we must become a single individual, family, society, nation, and world. Even if we cannot become a single nation or a single society, we must become a single self. If we do so, the nation will look up to us, and all people will admire us. 
When we work and fight in such a position, faith is born. The word must be put into practice. All of you gathered here are from the Seonghwa Student Association and have become connected with the 7th or 3rd graduates. Connections are not something to be severed; rather, you carry the burden of this connection without realizing it. 
Now, when you leave this place, you will part ways in all directions. You will scatter to Gyeonggi-do, Chungcheong-do, Jeolla-do, or Gyeongsang-do. The farther you go, the more your longing for the center of connection will increase. A person feels more attachment to their homeland after leaving it. Going far does not mean that the connection is severed. The farther you go, the deeper the emotional connection becomes. 
People strive to establish goodness on this earth, and if they have dedicated something, they will work to connect with it even more. Even when leaving their homeland, they gather related materials and content. The same goes for leaving this earth. The question is, what will you take with you? Becoming a single existence is about preparing what you will take with you. If you become a single existence in your family, you will receive the blessings of that family; if you become a single existence in your nation, you will receive the blessings of that nation; if you become a single existence in the world, you will receive the blessings of that world. 
You are not going alone. When facing members who are fighting alone in the region, the desire to fight together arises because we are bound by an unbreakable connection. The Unification Church is now fighting to achieve the purpose of a single individual, a single family, and a single creative entity. 
If you have sorrow, it is not just personal sorrow. The same goes for the family. The sorrow of the family is not just the sorrow of the family. The Unification Church, too, is not just a church but is grieving centered on the cosmic purpose and emotional connection. God has a history that has led the one existence He wanted to bless into sorrow, pain, and the cross of death due to human betrayal.

In other words, a religion that has the idea of unity must emerge.

The Unification Church is the religion that has come forth with such an idea and to fulfill such a mission. All of humanity is that person. Our bodies are that person. Our hearts are that person. The one who can say this is the coming Messiah. The place where we gather to prepare to welcome that person is the Unification Church.

From this perspective, the people of the world are very pitiful. Each person may not seem that way when looking at themselves, but the reality is that it is so. Then, how far are you from such a world? There is absolutely no way to reach that world through worldly methods. However, no matter how much a thief may be, if they hold onto this absolute standard and weep, they too will become a citizen of heaven. The place that takes such people and makes them weep is precisely the Unification Church. To do this, one must be conquered. To be conquered, one must let go of oneself.

A person must originally have the mouth of nature, the head of nature, the eyes of nature, and the ears of nature, and must be nourished by the milk of nature. Yet, there is not a single person like that. Everyone is a zero-point human. Looking at such humans is a sight that is hard to bear. Therefore, God is carrying out the providence of restoration to create humans who are not like that. Our Unification Church must serve as a messenger for this purpose.

The Savior is the one who introduces the Creator, the Lord of heaven and earth. You must want to see that person, want to go to that person, and want to live with that person. Looking at the condition of humanity, one can see that the end has come. At this time, the place you want to go for eternity is heaven.

The place that remains as our hope is the homeland. Everyone wants to go to their hometown. The longing for the homeland exists because the original person lives there. The one we infinitely want to see, like our parents in our hometown, is God. So, is it enough just to see? No. We must live together. There is a bond that we must live together with God.

What is the thing we miss most from our hometown? The thing we miss most is our parents, but we must first miss our siblings. Those siblings are the believers in the religious world. Therefore, believers should not fight among themselves. They must cooperate and rely on each other. Those parents can be the parents of black people, yellow people, white people, and multicolored people. The world that is formed centered on those parents is heaven. Although this earth may be like a speck of dust among celestial bodies, it can become heaven. 

Let us establish that country and serve the Father

The family is the basic unit for the completion of heaven. Heaven is a place that, once visited, one does not want to return from, and where one wants to meet again and again, no matter how many times. If all people want to go there, want to see that being, and want to live with that being, the world will be unified. The Unification Church is moving toward that. However, it is not something that happens all at once. First, the expectations of individuals must be established, then the expectations of families, and then it must extend to nations, states, and the world.

However, if we meet without expectations being established, it can only be sorrowful. Children and parents will feel wronged. Therefore, there must be a movement to fight and take back what belongs to the enemy, on behalf of the sorrow of parents and siblings.

So, what does the Unification Church do? It is a place to turn upside down the satanic world that has been God's enemy for 6,000 years.

Now that we have come here and know that Father and the circumstances of heaven that established that Father, we can only face it with tears. We have a mission as the chosen people to do such things. We must fight with our lives on behalf of our parents and siblings. Only then can we fulfill the mission of our elder brothers.

You have been called to create such people. To fight on behalf of heaven may seem pitiful on one hand, but on the other hand, it is an indescribably happy thing. If Korea becomes the center of that fight and the world surrenders, how happy would that be? Since you are in such a place, you must become people whom no one can dare to lead away. You must establish an absolute standard that cannot be led away even by your own parents.

For that world, we must serve the Father and create a world that can be eternally glorious. Therefore, no one can dare to command me. The only one who can give commands is that being alone. However, since Satan has made it this way, we must subdue that enemy and fulfill our will to create the kingdom of hope. Can you do that?

To do this, you must pack your bags and set out again. This intention is my hope, the hope of the Savior, and the hope of God. The purpose of the Unification Church and your purpose in coming to the Unification Church is to fulfill these three hopes all at once. When this purpose is fully realized, the kingdom of hope, the heavenly kingdom of hope will be established.

Purpose of the dedication ceremony

<Summary of the words> Unity, this is God's hope. I and the other, and the whole world must become one. Our hearts must become one with God, and God's inner heart must be realized externally.

The issues are individual, family, tribe, and nation. We must pass through seven stages from the individual to the cosmos. We must always think about whether our hearts are one with God, whether our bodies are one with God, and whether our families are united centered on God.

Blessed families must have their hearts united with God, their bodies united with God, and their wills united with God. Only then can they become families that carry out the ideal of creation. Without families, a nation cannot determine its value.

Within each of us lies God's heart and hope. We are the embodiment of God's heart. We are in the position of representing God's will.

We must connect individual joy to the joy of the cosmos. My will must become our will and the will of the whole. We must be centered on myself, centered on us, and become one. Since we have inherited the bloodline of the fall, there remains a connection to the fall in this world. Here, we must create an expectation of victory.

The family is the smallest unit representing the whole. A mistake in this unit is a mistake for the whole. Individual mistakes can be forgiven through connection, but family mistakes cannot be forgiven. The heart that seeks to make individual joy the joy of the whole must be full.

We must discard personal circumstances, perspectives, and hopes, and establish the circumstances, perspectives, and hopes of the whole to merge into something greater. The family exists to save the whole. Therefore, the family is like a transmission line. Through the family, we must be able to harmonize with the whole. Therefore, the trinity must live in one house. Now is the time to reorganize the family.

Before the Teacher, there remains a global struggle to find God's sovereignty, God's people, and God's land. This is the mission of the Teacher who has come to this land. Centered on this, becoming a loyal subject and a filial child is the second mission, and creating an environment where one can act without being separated is the third mission.

We must hold a dedication ceremony based on these three missions. To do this, we must create holy sites. Thus, we must be able to unite around this and connect with heaven. To do this, the Teacher must find the standard that represents God and stands in the place of Jesus and the Holy Spirit. Only after that can we hold a dedication ceremony.

Until now, God has worked through all things, then through children, and then through parents. When this reverse order is turned around, it connects directly to heaven centered on True Parents in a flat standard. We must at least turn around on a national standard.

Now is the time to turn around. However, we cannot turn around without the name of the True Parents. Also, families cannot turn around without the names of loyal subjects and filial children. We must undergo internal renewal.

In the future, there will come a time when you cannot participate in this ceremony if you want to. What you have sworn in your life centered on family and individual life is for the cosmos, and without establishing a standard that can please the cosmos, you cannot turn around.

When you turn around, is there land that can be called God's? Is there a ship? Is there an airplane? This event symbolizes that.

The Teacher has borne the responsibility of turning history alone. To take on such responsibility, one must have a desperate heart. If there is someone who wants to unite with a king who has lost sovereignty and is living in a miserable state, on the day that king regains his authority, all people will bow their heads to that person.

I have nothing. My body and everything are not mine. I must establish a family and a global foundation on which I can stand. All of this must unite to hold a dedication ceremony. The vertical standard of heart must be established horizontally.

Who must we be representatives of? Who went this path first? Until now, it has not mattered if we have failed in our endeavors, but from now on, it must not be that way. We must not mock offerings. It is the era of the restoration of all things, so we must hold a dedication ceremony and turn around. We must abandon the thought of "my things" and "my family" and adopt the mindset of "the Father's things."

During this period, there will be no one among the blessed who dies. I have prayed, worrying that the children might go astray. Until now, I could not pray for blessings for the church. I also could not say, "Father, come here." This is because I have not been able to prepare a place where the Father who has come cannot be sent back like Jesus.

We must go down. Let us become naked. When we weep from a position of injustice, God will come to us. We must stand in a position where Satan cannot accuse us, no matter what we do. Even if I die, I must be able to say that I have established a spiritual watchman, so this place cannot be accused by Satan. The blessed people must establish this standard so that the kings of the world will dedicate their nations.

In the past, women could not enter the sanctuary. Because I have blessed families after passing personal tests, the era of personal indemnity has passed.

Today is a day of judgment for all. To pray for children to inherit the good qualities of their parents, one must accumulate sufficient achievements. Until now, we have not been able to establish the conditions on earth to ask for blessings, but that time is coming.

If you do not become like Kim Sat-gat, I will become like that. The next three years will be another period of hardship. The period in which you cannot raise your head is a three-year period. You must live a life of bowing your head like a sinner.

You must establish a standard by which the world can weep and pass through. If you do not establish that standard, the Teacher will be accused. Only after establishing three or more people who weep with tears and try to stop you will Satan not accuse you.

The Teacher has not been able to raise his head until now. In the future, the blessed people will not be allowed to remain at headquarters. Instead, others must be allowed to be there. Jesus could not raise his head for 2,000 years. The blessed did not receive rewards. This is because it is to give family rewards.
Through such a dedication ceremony, what belongs to the teacher must exist for the family members to come into being. Since we cannot offer everything, we must at least establish one-tenth and move forward. All of you must participate in this procession. The entire church must settle and move on. Let’s resemble the Father
<Summary of the message> I would like to express my gratitude to all of you who have guided the trainees and to the trainees who have endured until the end despite unfavorable conditions. I believe that during your training, you have made a solemn inner resolution. The title of the message I want to share with you today is "Let’s resemble the Father."

A Father who works hard
In this world, there are many pitiful and miserable people, such as the poor, those who suffer, those who despair, and even those who take their own lives. However, compared to those who live for the will of heaven, their difficulties are trivial. God is a sorrowful being. In the beginning, God had servants, the true parents He would establish, and all things. God was supposed to preside over all of this and be immersed in infinite happiness. However, God lost all of this. Rather, these things became enemies before God and objects of sorrow. Of course, individuals, families, nations, and the world must all be sorrowful, but God experienced the entire misery all at once.

God has come out, having lost the beloved servants, children, the family He cherished, and heaven on May 10, 1963 (Friday), from the former headquarters church. You must realize that while the sorrow of losing such things is great, you must also understand that God has stood before the cross after losing them. 

We must not forget that within each of us, there is a connection between the sorrow of the individual and the sorrow of the entire universe. We must also not forget that God possesses a universal foundation. God has come out with sorrow. Moreover, He has also taken on the responsibility of restoration. From that standpoint, He has been dealing with us until now. God has come out bearing the responsibility for human restoration even amid infinite sorrow. We must recognize that He has not only taken on the overall responsibility for the physical world, the spiritual world, and all of humanity but has also fought against Satan. It is difficult enough to take on responsibility, yet God has also fought against Satan. We must understand that He is a sorrowful Father who struggles to overcome obstacles and seeks restoration.

The history of 6,000 years until now has been the foundation laid by the Father in the era of the servant for the era of the children. The ideal of the Second Coming is to eliminate the sorrows of the servant, the sorrows of the children, and even the sorrows of the parents. Why do we subjugate the servant and establish the son to serve the parents? This is to establish individuals, families, and restoration standards to eliminate sorrow. To do this, the ideal of the Second Coming is centered around the reality of hope.

The returning Lord comes to take responsibility for history. The Lord must endure the persecution of the servant, the persecution of the children, and even the persecution of the false parents. Initially, the servant betrayed, the children betrayed, and the parents betrayed. Therefore, to restore this, we must bear the sorrow of the parents and achieve victory, not turning that victory into a personal victory but into the victory of the children, the victory of a central figure, the victory of heaven and earth, and the victory of all creation. Without this, the sorrows of the entire universe will not come to an end.

Just as the Lord does not claim the glory of victory for Himself but turns it over to God, we too must not claim the glory of our victories for ourselves but must turn it into the glory of heaven, the glory of the nation, the glory of the family, and the glory of our descendants. Only then can we become citizens of heaven. The Father fought and won from the position of a servant, even while holding the authority, taking on sorrow, so we too must stand in such a position.

The returning True Parents must walk this path as well. All of your lives and activities after training must be aimed at establishing this one purpose. You must be those who take responsibility, fight, and achieve victory. Because there are historical ties remaining, you must inherit this and take responsibility for the past and present, as well as the future.

In some respects, you could say that you have a greater responsibility than God. This is because while God has the responsibility of creation, we, who are in the era of shared responsibility among saints, have the responsibility to fulfill the will of the present and the future. We must realize that we have a responsibility greater than God as we transition into the era of the children.

Our Responsibility
God created all things, and we humans are to govern the created things, and God governs us humans who govern all things. Today, this era demands people who will take responsibility for the sorrow of God and fight against it. 

You do not know how great your responsibility is, as you must fulfill the responsibility of the True Parents toward the world. Just because we are on God's foundation, we cannot be complacent. We must move forward with a firm confidence that we will fight and win against Satan.

You are in a position where you must fight and win in a world governed by Satan. I have this global responsibility. I have the historical connection that God has worked hard for over 6,000 years, and I must think about whether I can stand before the heart of God in this historical context.

If we cannot take on the burden with concern, we must conquer it through struggle. We have said we want to resemble the Father and learn from the Father, so we must become those who take on the Father’s sorrow more than anyone else. Our Unification Church calls for us to fulfill our human responsibilities toward families, nations, and the world. We must take responsibility.

The time has come when everyone who has entered the world of the spiritual and physical realms, as well as all those who have come into the world of morality, must cooperate. In the past, cooperation from the spiritual realm was not possible. If cooperation was done incorrectly, it would lead to severe losses. In the past, cooperation was done through Jesus.

Now, since the First Israel and the Second Israel are cooperating, we can be concerned and fight for the will. We must also be concerned and fight for the First and Second Israel. If we fight and win for the individual, the personal era will pass; if we fight and win for the family, the family era will pass; if we fight and win for society, the societal era will pass; if we fight and win for the nation, the national era will pass.

In the past, because a flat standard was not established, even a small mistake could lead to the loss of a position. In other words, the foundations of the individual, family, society, nation, and world would disappear.

Now, you are within the privilege of moving toward a higher place. How happy is this? It is a great happiness to be able to engage in hopeful concerns that do not end in sorrow.

Having understood the connection with heaven, you must establish a certain relationship during the remainder of your life. I, as an individual, must carry the sorrow of heaven and live for the family, the nation, and humanity. The people of heaven are in a position to work hard to love all things. Therefore, they are very busy.

You must feel regret for having lived without value in the past. Now, how happy it is that God is entrusting you with the battlefield, the will, and the command!

In the past, you could only stand on the basis of the servant or the adopted child. But now, you are in a position to directly resolve everything. How happy is this? When we take on concerns and responsibilities, it becomes not just for the family but for the nation and humanity, which is a great happiness!

If we wish to resemble the Father, we must understand how the Father has fought for 6,000 years. During the time of Jesus, He endured suffering beyond death for the sake of the Son.

How happy you are to be able to work for the True Parents in this age of the Second Coming!

We have started with the content of the three eras. God has also gone through the era of the servant, crossed the 40 hills, passed through Golgotha, and is now in the position of walking the three-day journey. You must endure suffering from the position of the servant, endure suffering from the position of the children, and endure suffering from the position of the parents who have crossed Golgotha.

The Path to Resemble the Father
The fortunes of the era have passed through the era of rebirth, the era of growth, and have reached the era of completion. In the era of completion, what came before will be cut off. The path of the will ahead will become increasingly easier.

As we move from the era of the parents to the era of the children, you will take on the responsibilities that the Triune God has been handling. When that happens, God will be able to hand everything over to humanity before Satan. At this time, you must unite and not succumb to the hardships and crosses of the three eras but achieve victory.

Thus, you must turn the glory of victory above to heaven and below to the parents. You must return to God the family, the nation, and the world that He desired. You must return not only the individual but also the family, the nation, and the world.

You are not going as individuals. We must be concerned and take responsibility. We must achieve victory. We must restore everything. And we must return all of that to the Father.

We must fight until the Father, who has received all of that, returns it to you as yours. You must clearly understand this and until that time, you must be concerned, take responsibility, and fight. This is the path to resemble the Father.

Until now, we have been preoccupied with trivial matters such as what to eat and what to wear. But from now on, we must think about more significant matters and be faithful in establishing traditions to inherit historical things. We must know that we must struggle to fulfill the providence of restoration while taking responsibility for historical ties. *

The Path I Must Take
You must always think about the history of restoration. If God were to call all of you gathered here and say, "I will entrust you with the responsibility of this world of death, and from now on, I will restore this world through you," what would you do? Have you thought about such things?

If you were to receive the command to take responsibility for the history of restoration, which God has worked hard for 6,000 years but has not yet concluded, a restoration that must be concluded, it cannot be done by God alone. It must be a collaboration of God, humanity, and all things. Heaven, earth, and humanity must unite. 

It cannot be done with just people, nor can it be done with just God. Only when God, humanity, and all things unite can the history of restoration be concluded.

What a tremendous issue this is… If you were to receive a command from God saying, "You, from now on, take responsibility for this great mission and carry out the history of restoration," what would you do? Our Unification Church members have been learning and practicing the principles until now, and what is the ultimate position we must feel? It is precisely this position.

The whole world is now trapped in the powers of death and darkness. There is not a trace of light that God can grasp in this realm of darkness. If you, who are in this realm of darkness, receive God’s call based on the hard work and sincerity you have put in, that would be a great blessing.

If God were to say to you, "Heaven, earth, and this world are all entrusted to you. The entire universe will be blessed because of you. I will give you this infinite blessing, so you must bear this responsibility," what position would you take?

God has come out to find humanity, starting from the individual to the family, society, nation, and the entire universe. God has expanded the scope of His providence for restoration in this way. Ultimately, God aims for the restoration of the circle that includes God, all things, and humanity, that is, complete restoration.

God has worked through individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world, but what is the ultimate purpose of this history? It is to ensure that all creation remains within the realm of the ideal creation that God desires.

This creation must be centered around a perfect individual. Only then can God be pleased, and all things themselves can also rejoice. The perfect individual who becomes the center must not be someone who stands alone, but someone who can make the whole take responsibility. This means that whatever that person does must represent the equal value of all beings in heaven and earth moving together to work. Only when such a valuable existence emerges can the overall purpose of God’s providence for restoration, that is, the providence of salvation, be achieved.

People are called the lords of creation, but what kind of people can be the lords of creation? Is it someone who lives only for their family, like you do now? Is it someone who claims to be responsible for society? Or is it someone who leads the two major factions of the world? No.

We need someone who can be entrusted with the entire heaven and earth. Entrusting does not mean handing over a well-established foundation built on all victories. It means entrusting the tremendous world of darkness, where the enemy’s hordes are spread out globally. Today, someone must emerge who carries the conviction to take responsibility for the world with this mission. Otherwise, this world cannot escape from the realm of danger.

Those who must bear this responsibility and mission are the believers who follow the will of restoration and those who are struggling to find the path of morality, yet has there ever been anyone who has received God’s call to take on this universal mission? Even if there has been, did that person fulfill that responsibility? This remains unresolved to this day. You must understand this.

What the Unification Church has Aimed For
So, what has the Unification Church aimed for, and what kind of people should we become in the future? In the face of this world, can you stand alone having received God’s call and say, "I will fulfill this global mission in this realm of darkness"? You must be able to say, "Father, I will do it. Please entrust me with everything." 

To that end, until now, the members of the Unification Church have gathered and moved and fought. 

Then, what is the fixed position we can ultimately remain in, the decisive position? While the whole world stands as an enemy, betraying God, I must stand in the position of having received the final command from God the Father and take on that responsibility. You must think about standing in such a position.

The history of restoration until today has been a history to find one person, Adam. It has taken 6,000 years to find one person, Adam. It has taken 6,000 years. It is not just one era, nor just one century. It is not a process within history. The entire history of humanity has been a history of restoration to find the lost ancestors. For 6,000 years, God has been working to find the lost Adam.
God intends to completely find this Adam, lay the foundation of victory, and then teach all humanity the principles of victory so that each individual can stand on a perfect foundation. Only then can everyone stand on such a foundation, believing that they have the standard to conquer the world, and in practicing that belief, they can finally establish the noun "completion." You must understand this. Do you understand?

Therefore, what we must always think about is how we would act if we were called before God without knowing heaven or earth, without anyone knowing anything at all. If we receive a command to fulfill such a mission in the midst of a dark world where we do not know what the principle is, except through the teachings of the Unification Church, we need to consider what kind of sense of responsibility, determination, and resolution we must carry with us.

Unless you stand in such a position, you cannot understand the circumstances of your ancestors, nor can you comprehend the historical connections of countless ancestors who have worked hard until now. From that perspective, you can say, "Ah, Noah was like this." In such a position, you can understand Noah's situation, who had to take responsibility and fulfill his mission at the family level, Moses' situation, who had to take responsibility in the national sphere on behalf of his tribe and nation, or Jesus' situation, who had to bear the tremendous mission of making the countless enemies of this world into God's sons and daughters, direct children. Standing in such a position allows you to understand who Jesus is.

Today, you, the members of the Unification Church, have also come out from such a position. A person who cannot comprehend such a position is irresponsible and not a normal person. They are limited to a certain field. However, you must understand the historical connections of heaven that have gone through such a process in this era, and you must have a burning heart of conviction to set the standard of victory and take revenge on the enemy.

That heart must not be temporary. You must have the conviction that you will build a blessed world by overcoming the terrible tribulations of this era, stepping on the history of the past. Only such a person can walk the path of faith without falling until the end; otherwise, no matter how much they try, they cannot go.

You who have entered the Unification Church today are learning the principles. You are learning the principles centered on the Adam family, the Noah family, the Abraham family, Jacob, Moses, and the era of Jesus, and you are learning about God, who has been guiding history from behind. However, you are ultimately beings who follow. Therefore, you must walk according to the principles without rest.

Thus, you should be able to say, "I will restore the Adam family, I will restore the Noah family, I will restore the Abraham family," and not only restore them but also command them. If you are to bear the global mission of being called by God in this dark world, you must stand in a position where you can say, "This is how Moses had to lead the Israelite nation."

The principle has no exceptions. You must become a person who can direct how the events that occurred during Jesus' life should be resolved if they were to occur in this era. In this era, you must take responsibility from the position of one who has received the call of heaven and has undertaken the mission of heaven. You must take responsibility from the standpoint of "it must be me."

You are still immature in front of the will. Now, what should we, the members of the Unification Church, possess? There is nothing in this world. It is the heart that says, "I am the only one left."

The principles are the same for everyone. In the path of restoration that humanity must take, it is all the same. The positions of Noah, Moses, Jesus, and the position of the teacher guiding you today are all the same. There cannot be a statement like, "Someone has a specific mission, so they must take that responsibility." There can be no exceptions. From a universally valid standpoint, everyone must stand in a position of responsibility. It is a problem if someone says, "Oh! This person is treated as an exception." It cannot be said, "It was because it was Jesus." Do not treat anyone as an exception. Here, everyone is equal and fair. There are no exceptions in the principles.

You must feel the tremendous mission to establish a standard that can overcome tribulations. The problem lies here.

Now, when you pray, try to do so in this way. You have learned the principles, yet you know nothing, nothing at all. What have you learned? Do you understand what the fall is? You stand in a position where you know nothing, but you must seek it out and take it back from Satan.

In that position, you must confront the historical enemy, Satan, under the standard of what a person should be, defeat Satan, and lay the foundation of victory in the current environment. With this foundation, even if you must endure all the tribulations and pains left in the world of Satan, you must stand peacefully, centered on the standard of heart, to establish a new world, that is, God's ideal world. Even if you are placed in the center of suffering, you must stand calmly with that foundation of heart. From that perspective, you must repent.

When have you ever felt the sorrow of Adam being cast out by God after the fall? Have you ever felt the heart of Noah, who, for 120 years, endured the harsh environment while biting his tongue, fearing that the will might not be fulfilled? You must be able to direct those who are in the same position as Noah, who was advised by God to go. You must be able to direct those who are in the same position as Moses. You must have the conviction that you can take on such responsibility and possess a natural value that allows you to stand before the universe and acknowledge yourself. It is not a forced value. Are you truly in a position where you can do that?

When viewed from the perspective of the Noah family, everything Noah did was not just personal but familial. What Abraham did was not just for himself but for the Abraham family. What Jacob did was not just Jacob's work. What he labored for over 21 years was not just for his own individual benefit but for his 12 brothers. The same goes for Moses. He worked for the hope of Israel.

Have you ever stood in such a position? Think about it. From now on, you must have such thoughts. If you have taken on such a mission without a teacher or a father, then it is a responsibility that must be fulfilled even if it means death. What will happen if you do not fulfill it?

Consider where you should begin. If you want to address the issues of the Adam family first but do not know how to solve the problems of that family, you cannot take action. However, if there is a teacher who brings the materials to solve those problems, how wonderful would that be?

Recently, I heard from a student attending a university that scholars go around collecting materials in their fields of expertise, and if there are global materials or more beneficial materials, they do not think about how they should conduct themselves to obtain them, but they desperately run around with all their might. The heart of scholars is to obtain those materials, even if it means giving up all their wealth for their field of expertise. Those who are in a position to study their field of expertise do not find anything too precious.

When you are in such a position, how will you gather the materials regarding the Adam family and take responsibility for solving all the problems of the Adam family? When you are struggling to solve those problems, how grateful would you be if a teacher came along with good materials and taught you how to do it?

You may not think so, but I have devoted my whole life to the value of the principles after understanding them. Each word of the principle is not something obtained by chance. It is a universal material that cannot be bought even for thousands or millions of dollars. It is a universal material that is connected throughout the world of heart. I thought that because I have the mission and responsibility to restore this world, if I do not find these principles, I will not achieve the purpose of being born as a human, and all humanity will fall into the abyss of death. When I think of such a tremendous problem, what do you think?

People from the past, including Noah's family, passed through without knowing these facts. But now that we know this, we must restore and align ourselves to stand in the position of God's representative.

God knows everything, but He could not teach that fact to humanity. You have learned the principles and understand, but God placed humans in such a position and hoped that humanity would seek out the truth themselves. How much did God want to teach that path? How desperate must God's situation have been that He could not teach it? What is the Unification Church teacher doing today? It is to solve these issues. There are historical grievances intertwined globally, and they must be resolved. If there are thorns on the path of the bridegroom, they must be cut away, and if there are mountain peaks, they must be leveled to create a solid path. Those who can do this are the apostles, but those who wish to become brides only want to eat the flesh and blood of the bridegroom; can that be acceptable?

What is the bridegroom before the bride? He is the man among men. The man among men! You may have heard of virtuous women, but have you heard of the man among men? Jesus was the man among men for all who became brides. Heaven and earth acknowledge Him, history acknowledges Him, the times acknowledge Him, and the present and future acknowledge Him as the man among men. Do those who wish to become brides before such a Jesus think they can even establish the noun of virtuous women? To say they will become the bride of Jesus without being virtuous women is robbery. What if a woman living in a beggar's den claims that President Kennedy is her husband? What would happen? Everyone would say she is crazy.

Christians are engaging in such nonsense. From a beggar's position, they are calling out to the Prince of God, "Oh, bridegroom, come quickly!" They are saying, "Come and live with me, Jesus," while wrapped in rags. That is why the sorrowful Jesus has not yet been able to resolve the grievances. Since Jesus could not resolve the grievances, do you think the grievances of the God who sent Jesus have been resolved? They have not. Since neither God nor Jesus could resolve the grievances, all of creation, which was made by God, could not resolve them either.

Therefore, we must resolve the grievances of heaven and earth, but how should we do that? The one who comes to resolve the grievances of the fall is the Messiah. To resolve grievances, we must resolve the grievances of all creation, the grievances of humanity who have not become God's true sons and daughters, and then we must resolve the grievances of the Holy Spirit, who has toiled on this earth and groaned. After that, the Messiah must resolve his own grievances. Only then can we finally resolve God's grievances. That is how the mission of the Messiah ends.

The purpose for which God sent Jesus
When Jesus came to this earth, He came with the purpose of resolving such historical grievances. He came as the embodiment of God's heart and the hope of God's historical desire, as God's representative. When God sent Jesus, He sent Him as the fruition of the hope of 4,000 years of history; thus, Jesus was the center of global restoration. Therefore, humanity centered on Jesus, all creation centered on Jesus, angels centered on Jesus, and the spirit world centered on Jesus, that is, everything will be realized on the day centered on Jesus, and only then can God finally live with humanity. This is the purpose for which He sent Jesus. Do you understand? The purpose of God sending Jesus to this earth was not to hold onto Jesus alone. He sent Jesus as the subject to find the original world after laying the victorious foundation for 4,000 years to find the original world.

Thus, the Jesus who came to the earth had the responsibility to resolve all grievances of creation, the grievances of humanity, historical grievances, temporal grievances, and future grievances, and after completely resolving His own grievances, He had to approach God and be united with God's love. This was the highest purpose of Jesus. Before He could settle the world, He could not have a relationship of love before God, which is the principle of creation. Therefore, Jesus came to this earth to achieve the principled goal. But did He settle the world when He came to this earth? Did He settle humanity? No, He did not. Did He settle all the sovereigns of this earth? No, He did not. He left behind the noun of judgment without having settled them.

This Jesus will return to this earth as the King of kings and settle everything, establishing the conditions for victory, resolving historical grievances, and presenting the entire world to the Father. The time for that will come to an end. Therefore, at the end of that time, Jesus must also resurrect. Now Christ has risen from the dead, the firstfruits of those who have fallen asleep. For since death came through a man, the resurrection of the dead comes also through a man. For as in Adam all die, so in Christ all will be made alive. But each in turn: Christ, the firstfruits; then, when He comes, those who belong to Him. (1 Corinthians 15:20-23) is what the Bible says, right?

Jesus must also resurrect. Everything is in the Bible. The first ripe fruit, Jesus, must also resurrect. What kind of resurrection? He must resurrect as a king who rules the world centered on God's heart, having shed the grievances of paradise and ruling as the king who governs heaven and earth in place of God.

We must look to heaven with our hearts and look down to the earth with our bodies. We must advance to the standard where this body and heart become one and can rule the world with love. Because such conditions remain, Jesus must resurrect. After that, those who belong to Christ, that is, the saints, must resurrect. Then comes the end, when He hands over the kingdom to God the Father after He has destroyed all dominions, authorities, and powers. (1 Corinthians 15:24) It is said, right? That time is the end. Let us think about Jesus' life before He fulfilled His purpose.
Once again, let us think about Jesus. Jesus came to this earth, leaving the heavenly throne, bearing the mission of restoration. What did Jesus have to do? He had the responsibility to restore all things, the responsibility to restore all humanity, the responsibility to restore the servants (angels), and the responsibility to restore children.

Therefore, He had to have the heart of a global parent among parents, the heart of an older brother among brothers, the heart of a filial son on a global scale, and the heart of a loyal subject on a global scale. He also had to have the heart of a global priest. And if there were ancestors who had accumulated good deeds before God through their loyalty on this earth, He had to have a loyal heart that did not fall short of theirs. That is why Jesus, while living in Jerusalem, would pray, "Oh God, I am eating this meal; please accept it as the three offerings that were offered on Abraham's altar."

Everyone, do you know the Bible? Can you read the Bible? It turns out that Jesus had such a heart. Why? Because He was to bear the global responsibility. Because of the fall, He had the mission to internally indemnify all conditions of groaning of all creation and humanity that had lost everything and were within the realm of groaning. Therefore, Jesus laid the foundation of such a historical life in silence.
I had to go out. Before he could express his intentions in the human world, he had to live in the world of my inner feelings, centered on the background of history, without anyone knowing. 

Although it seems that he lived carelessly and laughed in the world for 30 years, his entire life was a sacrifice. Everything he saw and heard was something that the Father could accept. 

My weeping is to connect with the Father’s suffering, and my movement is to offer this land, this wicked world, as the Father’s. 

He lived with that standard. Thus, he had the absolute purpose of establishing a relationship with all things on this earth. 

You must understand this. Jesus had a heart that wished for the sins of all people to be atoned for, whether asleep or awake. Even when he went to bed, he carried the heart that wished for the sins of all people to be atoned for. In the quiet night, he would wake up and pray alone, fulfilling the priestly mission of offering sacrifices on behalf of all people. 

“Father, please accept me as your substantial being to indemnify the conditions of universal sorrow.” He lived a hidden prayer life. 

What has God lost? God has lost His servant. He has also lost all things and His children. Therefore, there had to be a preparation period for Jesus to be accepted as a good substitute for all things before God, and then there had to be a period of serving as a servant before God, and a period of filial piety as a son. 

However, Jesus left behind the title of a filial son but could not leave behind the title of a loyal subject. He had to stand in the position of the archangel of this world, restore the world, and move forward as the Son of God. He had to be loyal in the position of the archangel before this earth and show filial piety in the position of the child of God. In other words, he had to become the one and only son of God and the one and only loyal subject. 

Therefore, if there are those today who wish to become brides on this earth, they must first subdue Satan remaining on the earth. That is fulfilling the mission of a servant. Thus, they must connect with Jesus, who fulfilled the mission of a son, and advance to the throne of God. When we look at Jesus’ life, he placed the value of all things in infinity and worked hard to resolve the grievances of all things. He also lived as the least of servants from the position of a servant. And he fulfilled the mission of the son among sons. 

Although he lived a short life of about 30 years, during that time he established the conditions for indemnity by taking on the entirety of restoration upon himself and by going up to Golgotha, he subdued Satan. However, the substantial world did not return to the realm of Jesus' ideals. Jesus only established the ideals of spiritual restoration. Thus, after leaving behind the term "Second Coming," he has been seeking the substantial world for the past 2,000 years. 

What did Jesus have to do during the three years of his public life? From the position of a servant, he had to restore from the individual to the family, from the tribe to the nation, to the world, and to the universe. He also had to restore from the position of a child from the individual to the world. Furthermore, he had to restore to the world with the heart of a parent. So what did Jesus do while he was alive? He worked to find the parents on behalf of the son using the body of a servant. 

During the three years of public life, he acted as a servant. This was because he had to fight against Satan as a servant. The archangel violated the heavenly law, so he had to subdue the angels and restore the position of the archangel. Since the archangel betrayed God as a servant, the three years of public life were the preparation period to restore the position of the betraying archangel. 

Through this three-year preparation period, he had to stand as the substantial being who restored the position of the archangel and fulfill the responsibilities of a son. Then what did he have to do? From the position of the victorious archangel, he had to establish the standard of restoration by setting up the bride. Thus, he had to stand in the position of the son. If there is a son of God, there must also be a daughter. Therefore, the man, Jesus, as the bridegroom, looks toward the woman, as the bride. Do you understand? This is because everything must be indemnified. 

In this way, Jesus had to complete the mission of the archangel during the three-year preparation period and complete the mission of the child. To complete the mission of the child, he had to create an environment where he could connect with his siblings and establish a foundation of brotherhood. Then he had to rise to the position of the parents centered on that foundation. 

To go to the position of the parents, there must be a bride and groom. Thus, the bride and groom must become the true parents of humanity as unfallen human ancestors. Here, the one who becomes the true father is Jesus. To stand as the true father of humanity on this earth, there must be a true mother. However, although Jesus completed the mission of the son, he could not find a bride to become the true mother. Therefore, he left behind only the spiritual connection of parents. Do you understand? 

Thus, Jesus, as the bridegroom, represents heaven, and the Holy Spirit, as the bride, represents the earth, establishing the standard of spiritual parents. Originally, a couple must be formed in reality and in a tangible way. This was the purpose that Jesus was originally meant to achieve. However, because it was only achieved spiritually, the spiritual and physical worlds could not unite. Therefore, the bridegroom, Jesus, ascended to heaven, and the bride, the Holy Spirit, came down to earth to work on uniting the spiritual and physical worlds again. Thus, all of humanity today is struggling within the realms of the spiritual and physical worlds. Do you understand? 

The world’s humanity does not know the motivation for this nor the purpose. They are like children who have not yet been born from their mother’s womb. Do you understand? You have been living while blinking your eyes and playing various games, but you are still in the realm of a baby who has not yet been born from the womb of the true parents. 

That is why people do not know how to live their lives. They do not know.

Do you understand? 

Earlier, I spoke of God’s love, but you are still in the womb, so you have not tasted God’s milk. You cannot see God’s face. Since you have not seen the face of your parents, it is like living in the womb. This is the situation that today’s humanity is in. Therefore, rebirth must happen. That is why He will come again. Right? He will resurrect and come back, right? Jesus, who crossed Golgotha, will come back as He went. Since He went with the cross, He will come back with the cross.

“I have fought this way. I will walk the path that Jesus walked as a servant. I will walk the path that Jesus left behind as a son.”
