May 22, 1963 (Wednesday), Headquarters Church.  
* This message was given on the last day of the three-year course (the end of the lunar month of April).

Now, we, the insufficient children, have returned before the Father. As we reflect on whether we can be called worthwhile children before your hard-earned image, the more we reflect, the more we find ourselves lacking. We cannot help but show our shameless and shameful selves, so please forgive us. Father, we earnestly wish and desire this.

Because you have not abandoned fallen humanity but have worked for 6,000 years to find and restore them, we have come before you with a heart of submission. We know that you have a heart that cannot abandon us and a deep longing to seek us out, and thus we have come before you today, calling you Father. Please forgive us.

We are lacking before the heart of the Father, who wishes for eternal sons and daughters with whom He can resonate, but please remember that our hearts long for you. We earnestly hope that you will have compassion on us, seeing the sincere desire in our hearts to stand before your image.

Father, we know that without you, we could not exist on this earth. Yet, we find ourselves in a position where we must once again express our reality that we are not living according to your will today. We earnestly wish and desire that you would forgive us, Father.

As we look upon the reality where Satan's authority remains on this earth, where unjust environments persist, and where the sovereignty of evil governs the entire universe, we, who are seeking Heaven, praising your will and calling upon your name, are in a position where we must lament our own shortcomings before you. Please have even more compassion on us.

Without your strength and protection, we cannot leave our existence on this wicked earth, nor can we leave anything before the providential will. We are insufficient beings, and we know this clearly from the facts that have manifested. Therefore, we earnestly ask you to add your heart of compassion once more and remember us.

Please admonish our disbelief and encourage us to walk the path of loyalty and filial piety, and fill our inadequacies so that we may gain the strength to come closer to perfection, Father. We earnestly wish and desire this.

On this day, May 22, 1963, the last day of the three-year course, reflecting on the many historical paths and observing the many phenomena of the times, we realize that we have the mission to lay the foundation for the historical recreation of the future. We have come to face this day, so please forgive us, Father.

Please forgive the sins of our ancestors, forgive the misfortunes of humanity today, and allow us to fulfill our mission to lay the foundation for eternal welfare for future generations, even though we do not know it. We earnestly wish and desire this.

Though we have been in such a position, we know that you have tirelessly worked to establish my individual self. It has come to the time when we must realize that it is because of my own insufficiency that the world has fallen into such a state today. It is not for any parent, nor for this world, but for my own self that you have walked this painful and arduous path. We know well that because of this, sad traces remain in the providential path you have walked.

Today, as we face the last day of the three-year course, reflecting on the day we made our vows and pledges before you, we cannot help but confess our unfaithfulness. Please forgive us. We have known your name, we have known your will, and we have called your name millions of times. Yet, was there ever a time when we could truly call you my Father? Was there ever a time when we stood before you, taking responsibility, saying this is my will? Was there ever a time when we struggled before you, vowing to confront the Satan of this world? We have been insufficient and lacking. We earnestly wish and desire that you would forgive us, Father.

Now, as we enter the last 40 days of this grace period, Father, please do not let your sons and daughters, who have been fighting for your will in various difficult environments throughout South Korea, lose heart. As we prepare to restart the historical path of the past, please fill these insufficient individuals with the internal elements of your strength so that they can create a new history. The Direction We Must Go
<Summary of the Message> It has been three years since you have established a new promise before God and pioneered the barren land of the three thousand ri (Korean measurement of distance).

We are at a turning point
Regardless of age, both the elderly and the young have gone through bloody struggles during this time. Various trials have blocked the way, but we have overcome them by thinking only of one purpose. We have paved the way with tears, blood, and sweat, unable to eat or wear.

When I first asked you to start the three-year course, I asked you to go as sinners. So for three years, I walked out as a sinner who was not a sinner. I know that you have fought to not be taken by Satan and not retreat. I also know that there are members who have fought even to the point of shedding blood to protect the mission.

You have worked hard in limited environments, but there was tremendous backing behind that effort. Moreover, that effort has prepared the way ahead, so from now on, it will become a foundation for establishing a new direction. Your movements may seem limited to individuals, but all those movements represent the historical devastation.

So, having completed this three-year period, what direction should we now go? Until now, the goal we have walked toward has been to lay the foundation for the nation. We have also made people aware that there is no other way for the 30 million people to survive. However, from now on, we must present the direction the world should go.

God governs individuals centered on families, families centered on nations, nations centered on states, and states centered on the world, universe, and heaven. Today is not the day to conclude providence but the day to start on a path of greater trials. When the Israelite people set out from the hardships of Egypt towards the path of freedom, there were actually greater trials ahead. However, the Israelite people, who did not know this, perished. That is, after destroying the seven nations of Canaan, they were supposed to establish a global standard, but because they did not know that, they perished.

Our Unification members have secured a foundation of victory during the past three years. Now we must lead this nation and lay a global foundation, and restore heaven and earth. To do this, we must not boast of our past loyalty but must offer new loyalty for greater things on this foundation. God wishes for this to happen. Previously, when meeting friends on the street, we bowed our heads due to environmental oppression. However, now that you have won in the struggle of the past three years, there is no longer a need to bow your heads. Now is the time for that.

If you have established a foundation that God can remember, a foundation of victory, then you must rise again and manage the environment. Otherwise, you will not be able to withstand future trials. At some point, you will perish. In a turning point, one side perishes while the other thrives. So what position will you take in this turning point? Will you be one who is removed, or will you be one who receives light and is reborn? This is the question.

The path of restoration must start from the individual and go until the kingdom of heaven is established. If the individual established by God cannot advance to the position of a family, God will raise up a new person to establish the foundation of the family and occupy that position. This is the heavenly law. The same goes for when a family rises to the national level. This is the progression of history. The same applies to you. If you cannot go from here to the world, others will dominate the world on the foundation you have laid. Until now, you have fought for the nation, but from now on, you must fight for the world.

We must lay a global foundation
We must put in our utmost sincerity. We must invest more than what we have for our own children, more than what we have for our families, and more than what we have for our nations. We must have a heart that cares for not only our nation but also the world, day and night. If foreign members are more numerous and more sincere than Korean members, the fortune will tilt towards them. Every time we hear news from abroad, we must resolve to not be outdone by them and continue on the path of victory to maintain heaven's fortune and to appear before them.

Until now, we have come out for individuals, families, tribes, and nations. However, from now on, we must go out centered on heavenly families. Blessed families must especially suffer. If you had not suffered during that time, you would not be able to sing the song of victory today. Even if you are a small existence that has not achieved anything worldly, you must set a standard that they can bow their heads and bend. From now on, you must suffer for the world, not just for your own tribe and race.

When you lay the foundation for the nation, God lays the foundation for the world. He always moves one step ahead. From now on, even people from Seoul must pack their belongings and go to the provinces. Just as God told Abraham to leave Ur of the Chaldeans without any excuses, you must leave in the same way. A natural migration must take place. Therefore, you must move voluntarily. In the future, there will be a large-scale migration of nations globally.

How should our Unification Church move forward? Having come this far...
I have come, but I cannot stay here. We are moving from an era where we can stay as individuals, families, ethnic groups, and nations to an era where we can stay globally. 
The most blessed people are the ancestors. To become an ancestor, one must become a historical figure. Those who have contributed for a long time in that area become the ancestors of that area. When God establishes an individual, He hopes that individual will establish a foundation that encompasses family, tribe, nation, and the world. 
What position is our Unification Church in today? What historical process are we in? What kind of period is this three-year period? Jesus bore the cross after a three-year course. Therefore, the period of laying the foundation for victory centered on the nation has collapsed. Thus, God's will has been extended, but it is not extended indefinitely. The 40 years of Japan-Korea annexation and the three years of military rule correspond to the 430 years of the Egyptian oppression in principle.

For the Unification Church, it was a year of making a life-and-death decision. By the teacher's marriage in 1960, the individual finally found a place. It was a pivotal point. What kind of pivotal point is it? It is like the pivotal point established during the three days before Moses crossed the Red Sea. Everything in the history of restoration is contained within this three-year period up to today. By completing this period, the proclamation ceremony for the registration of the association was held on April 13 of the lunar calendar, centered on the expectation of the son-in-law that was realized. 
When we need to transition to the family level, the marriage and dedication ceremony should have been completed within April. Because this was not finished, we must extend it. For this, the teacher prayed three days in advance. Without establishing this standard and transitioning, we cannot raise a new history. 
Originally, one cannot cross this path, this hill, as an individual. One can only cross it centered on the standard of a blessed family. Various blessings must be given. Everything must be done to cross over. Only then can one become a person who surpasses the standard of blessing. To do this, we must determine the holy ground and establish and commend those who represent heaven and earth. Based on this expectation, we must open the path of blessing. 
Those who pass through the spirits also visit our holy ground. This is because the holy ground is where heaven and earth meet. Nothing can be done without the sons and daughters of God. 
The tears shed at the holy ground have become a standard that God can remember, which is why we hold the dedication ceremony. Once this ceremony is completed, I believe the way ahead will be opened greatly. 
<Prayer> Father, behind us are our beloved family members and the nation. Behind the nation is the world where Satan is active, but everything must become one in your love, Father. We must restore this world to establish connections of your love. 
We must find the True Parents, and we thank you for establishing them. We also thank you for establishing true sons and daughters. May the flags raised be a source of pride throughout the universe, and may they remain as a victory for all time, reviving humanity and heaven and earth. We thank you for allowing us to conclude the three-year course victoriously in April 1963. 
Please allow the 120 couples and the dedication ceremony to be established within April, and even if this period is extended, may Satan not invade. Amen. 
Blessed families must fulfill the roles of Jesus and the Holy Spirit. 
<Summary of the Message> The wives of district leaders must perform the role of secretary. The district leaders' wives have the responsibility for the revival of the district. They must leave behind achievements that show they have worked hard to establish the emotional foundation of the following family members. 
Blessed couples must fulfill the roles of Jesus and the Holy Spirit. The suffering of blessed people is due to the inability of those below them to support them. Therefore, we must work to instill the awareness that blessed families should not suffer. We must make them aware that if they cause suffering to blessed families, they will be punished. 
Without establishing a family foundation, a global foundation cannot be established. The age of saints refers to the family age. 
Due to the fall, the sun could not act as a beloved daughter before God, could not act as a sister before Adam, and could not act as a wife. Therefore, the teacher had to raise the mother like a daughter, love her as an older brother, and accept her as a bride. Because of the fall, the person who is to become a mother cannot have false parents or false brotherly love. 
The reason for choosing the mother at the end of April (lunar, solar) was explained. The mother must be like a sister, like a wife, and like a daughter. No matter how difficult things may be, there should not be family or relatives to whom one can appeal, such as one's own parents or older brothers.

Ultimately, all traditions must be established while the teacher is present. 
<Public Life and Blessing> 
<Summary of the Message> To achieve the purpose of creation that humanity desires, our actions must be good. Goodness is public. God is a public being. What is related to God is public. 
God is eternal. Therefore, what is limited cannot be said to belong to God. It is a natural phenomenon to want to leave behind goodness. 
We must have a thorough concept of the public. All aspects of life must be public. However, our Unification Church members have a weak public consciousness. Every action must be governed by public laws. 
Conscience aims for good places and good things. What is more public than the individual is the family, and what is more public than the family is the tribe, and what is more public than the tribe is the nation, the world, and the universe. Although we are individuals, our minds and passions must not remain with ourselves. 
God is the highest public being who is with us. We must embody God's love and God's essence. Sovereignty and people are all public. Only after being publicly recognized globally can we act freely on a national level, and only after being publicly recognized nationally can we act freely on a tribal level. 
Because we stand in a public position, if we fail to take responsibility here, we will suffer. We must recognize this responsibility and fight for the public good.

Three years have passed, and another half year is passing, so all important matters must be completed by July. 
God blesses the family after blessing the individual, blesses the tribe after blessing the family, blesses the nation after blessing the tribe, and blesses the world after blessing the nation. When wishing and praying to have children, we must pray for sons and daughters who will serve heaven and the nation. If we cannot make those who claim to be great suffer, our path will be blocked. 
<Significance of the Dedication Ceremony> 
<Summary of the Message> Before God created the universe, He already had ideals. This is based on God's heart. To realize that ideal before creation, God intended to establish the purpose of creation in the holy heaven and holy earth, that is, the new heaven and new earth. Based on that foundation, He wanted to establish a world of heart that fulfills the purpose of creation and establish an unchanging will of God on that foundation, centering on that will to bless. 
God's ideal centered on humanity 
This blessing is not only for humanity. It is also not only for heaven and earth. God blessed everything by investing everything from the foundation of His inner heart. If this blessing had been realized, this world, this universe, would have been filled with the glory of victory. In such a world, humanity, who embodies all the contents of God's heart, would have established a family foundation that pleases God and accepted the heavenly achievements as human achievements to build an eternal and unending happiness. This is God's ideal and wish. 
However, due to an unexpected mistake by human ancestors, the unfortunate event of the fall occurred, resulting in suffering in the world of humanity, and all humanity lost the homeland of welfare and began to live in a world of suffering. Therefore, it is natural that God, who looks upon this world, is saddened, and all creation, which was created by God, also mourns. 
To escape this sorrow, humanity must establish conditions for indemnity. To establish this condition, humans live in the world of death, repeatedly going through the history of indemnity. 
Because God is love, He cannot leave such humans in the world of death. With His deep and wide love, He came to restore His original will. Thus, a long history of six thousand years of blood and tears has flowed in search of lost children. During these six thousand years, historical sorrow has accumulated, the foundation of death has become more solid, and the entanglement of God's circumstances and human circumstances has become indescribably complicated. 
Looking at the children who are wandering the path of death, suffering from the mockery of enemies, God has been working in providence while confronting the enemies to protect humanity. This path of providence was not smooth. When humans suffer on thorny paths, they must be cleared, and when they struggle on paths of tears, those paths must be cleared, and when they are on bloody paths, those paths must be opened, and when there are groups moaning in places of death, those paths must be opened. 
We must not forget that God, who looks at the whole, regards the sad circumstances of each individual as the suffering of the entire world. From this perspective, no matter how great the sorrow in life may be, it is insignificant compared to God's sorrow. We must understand how great God's sorrow, God's injustice, and God's anger are. The sorrow of losing a child and the sorrow of a nation being destroyed and sovereignty being lost, when combined, cannot compare to God's historical sorrow. 
Then, what is my existence today? I am a being that adds sorrow to God. I am a being exchanged for God's sorrow. We must not forget that we are beings who have come to give and find God's sorrow. We who stand here are beings who have come to give God's sorrow, beings exchanged for God's sorrow, and beings who have come to give and find God's sorrow. If you forget this, you will not be able to rise above the historical wave of death. 
God is raising and caring for such me, finding a place of victory. The sorrow that arises from me does not end with me alone. I must remember that I have parents above me, siblings in front and behind me, a spouse on my left and right, and children below me. 
God's sorrow extends beyond me to my opposing parents, spouse, siblings, neighbors, compatriots, and all humanity, reaching to the ends of the earth. This sorrow cannot be turned back to God. If I do not have the conviction that I must take responsibility, I will have no face to stand before the Father. 
You have endured such a difficult path until now. You may have endured with the purpose that this is the only way I can survive, but you must endure with the thought that I endure for the Father's sorrow, that I endure to remove the Father's sorrow. As we struggle and suffer with this heart, as the time approaches us more and more, we must work diligently to fulfill our responsibilities and missions, forgetting sleep and the joy of life, so that we can stand before God. 
The responsibility of true children 
Considering this gathering on the day of dedication, this is a place of tears and a place of blood. It is a place of tears that cannot be stopped no matter how much we cry, a place of wailing that cannot be blocked by anything. What can we bring to such a place? We must have secrets in our hearts that others do not know. It is not about offering external objects, but about having deep-seated resentment and anger in our hearts. We must possess infinite value that cannot be exchanged for thousands or millions of dollars. We must be able to confirm this and be willing to bear the responsibility to achieve it. When this heart arises from your feelings, God can finally inherit the sorrow of six thousand years to you. 
Then, what kind of place is this today? It is a place where we solemnly inherit all of God's sorrow. Therefore, let us establish the original parents, original children, and original creation that the Father intended to establish, and offer them back to the Father with joy! One must have the conviction to lay the foundation to do this to qualify to attend here. I urge you to remember this again. 
God fought to find His children and all creation, to establish the world of original nature, and to inherit eternal and holy achievements to enjoy joy forever and ever. We must understand that even in sorrow, God wants to bless us even more. Therefore, you are new sons and daughters before His will, and you must be established as true families, true couples, and true children, becoming great beings who govern all creation. You must become true children who can enjoy the glory of eternity granted to you and fulfill the mission of welcoming the coming True Parents. You must allow the True Parents to rest and then unite with them to allow God to rest. Only then will the good God be the king of all creation.
It means that as our Father, He will reign and the kingdom of goodness will be established on earth.  
We must create such a kingdom and offer it to God. We must become the people of goodness before our Heavenly Parent, and we must offer all things to God, who is our Heavenly Parent. We must recognize that we have this responsibility. Humanity lost these things due to the fall of the human ancestors, so it is our duty to complete the mission of restoration, establish the kingdom before the Father, and become the citizens of the kingdom who offer all things. Only then can this world become one, governed as a single nation under one center.

Today, we must symbolically and figuratively fulfill all these conditions and, based on that foundation, establish true children centered on True Parents, serving God and connecting with Him. From that foundation, when we establish God's Day, Parents' Day, Children's Day, and All Things Day, and connect them in a flat manner, the world will become one, humanity will be one people, and one brotherhood. Thus, we must fulfill the ideal world of goodness that God envisioned at the time of creation. For this purpose, God created all things and established humanity as the subject of all things to fulfill His great purpose through humanity. However, because humanity fell, we must go through the path of restoration to realize the ideal world of creation.

The value and importance of public life  
The fact that we can reach such a stage in our generation is undoubtedly something to be celebrated not only by you but also by the 30 million people of this nation, the 3 billion people living on this earth, the hundreds of billions of spirits in the heavenly realm, and even the descendants who will come after thousands of years.  
So, on this day of the dedication ceremony, you must establish all conditions and, before the Father who is saddened by the absence of a nation, a people, and a territory, know that from now on, the children of God who can form the citizens of the kingdom will arise, and those children will create families, unite families to form nations, and lay the global foundation for history. Rejoice, for this will happen.

Today, centered on our Unification Church, we have laid the foundation for the primary victory religiously and have now proclaimed the secondary start through the blessing ceremony. What is the central content we have proclaimed in this nation until now? It is our truth and blessing. There is nothing else. We have declared this through blessed families. Thus, having gone through the first, second, and third stages, being able to proclaim this as a national grand event means that we have entered into a historical privilege of forming a relationship with the nation in building the kingdom of heaven in the future.

When we think about this, we can understand how significant today's dedication ceremony is. You must deeply engrave this in your hearts and recognize that everything you possess is not truly yours. The house you live in is not yours, and the food you eat is not yours. You must not forget that all these are public goods related to the eternal God. They are public goods. Even the clothes you wear and your living tools, as well as your very bodies, are not yours but public.

What is sin? It is the violation of these public goods.  
We, the Unificationists, must have a thorough attitude under this ideology. Everything belongs to God, so everything is sacred. Since all things are sacred, we, who live by consuming all things, are also sacred. Moreover, since all things possess infinite value, we, who own and live by them, also possess infinite value. Thus, as infinitely valuable and public beings, we must establish public families with public value.

Based on families, we must advance to tribes, based on tribes to nations, and from nations to the world, understanding that the small must be absorbed and become offerings for the greater good. We must live with the mindset that God's nation is our nation, God's people are our people, and God's possessions are our possessions. This is the mindset we must have, living in harmony with God's heart. The creation itself desires us to live and exist on this foundation of heart. Therefore, treating others without heart becomes a sin.

Today, when we treat all humanity as brothers, we must include God in our interactions and connect with God's heart. You must become those who treat material things with God's presence and heart as a model for your lives. Because God is a public being, He always addresses the whole. Therefore, violating the public is an act of rebellion against God.

However, it remains a stark fact that our ancestors violated God's public heart in Eden, and the archangel did the same. Knowing this, we must respect the sovereignty of all nations and all beings through heart when dealing with the tangled matters of creation and humanity. Only then will God work upon our actions. When we stand on such a living foundation, Satan cannot help but be consumed. We must not forget that the first weapon to organize and judge the enemy Satan is heart.

On this occasion, you must understand God's sorrow, and the greater God's sorrow, the more fervently He desires to bless us. Those of you in the process of restoration must first serve True Parents and then reconnect that relationship to restore the heavenly world. From this perspective, God's heart is to give you the inheritance of heaven and earth, the universe, and all humanity. Therefore, you must fulfill your mission as true sons and daughters in place of God and True Parents, preparing a foundation where you can be recognized as true children who can stand before God.

You must understand that if you do not accomplish this great cosmic task, you will not be able to show your face in the heavenly world. Knowing this, I earnestly ask you to dedicate your lives to fulfilling this mission as we celebrate today's dedication ceremony.

Who am I?  
<Summary of the message> At your age, you likely have many dreams and great hopes. You may have a burning desire and ambition not to fall behind others in anything. In this sensitive time, when you can adapt well to anything, you may also suffer while longing for the unknown world.  
The title I want to speak to you about today is "Who am I?"  
Who am I? Whose son am I, and to which path (do) I belong, and from which country do I come? My individuality cannot exist beyond relativity. Young people like you, who have aspirations, cannot exist without a counterpart.  
There must have been something better than what I have before I was born, and I want to place this better thing in my environment, in my family, and in my nation. When I seek something better but my environment does not meet that expectation, I cannot help but feel frustrated. If you have a desire for something better, you are happy people; if not, you are unhappy people. Those who can relate to something better will be able to live a progressive life.  
When I touch something with my hands or see something with my eyes, I want to touch something better and see something better. This is because I want to connect with something better. However, when that is absent, I naturally rebel and complain. Therefore, I must ignite the spirit to create something better in the hearts of the youth with my own hands.

We young people should not despair that there is nothing of better value but should live with the conviction to create something more valuable. When we live like this, we will nurture a second hope and be able to develop toward that hope. We must have the conviction to recreate the decaying branches of youth and organize the environment.  
Among those who have come here, some may have overcome opposing environments. You have flowed through various environments to get here, but from now on, let us create a better and more valuable environment with God's creation ideology.  
The fallen descendants live within the realm of lamentation. You must have the conviction to create a foundation of goodness within this realm of lamentation. To create greater goodness, you must have the conviction to trample down the wrong environment and fight. When you act proactively like this, even the evil environment will be absorbed into a good environment. This is the second creation.

No matter what environment you encounter, no matter how fierce the waves may be, if there are many people with the conviction to overcome them, this nation will not perish. The teacher also fights with this conviction.  
To recreate, one must not stand in a relative position but must become a subjective being standing in a subjective position. The student council cannot develop because it lacks the value of recreation. If you fall along the way, you will ultimately perish. Have you set a goal for recreation and marched forward? From where? You must start with yourself. You must recreate yourself as one who creates goodness and represents goodness.  
You, if there are those who have been recreated, raise your hands. There seems to be no one. Then, those who have the confidence to recreate, raise your hands.  
Who am I? I am a being who can establish goodness or break goodness. I am at a crossroads. If I want to fulfill the desire for something better, I must stand in the position of the object before God. Let us become those who defend goodness on this earth. And let us become those who hate evil.  
What does God want to be good first? He wants your own hearts to be good. Then, what is a good heart? It is a heart that is full of affection and wants to embrace anyone. A heart that sympathizes when seeing others in difficulty is goodness. A heart that explodes with righteous indignation and wants to cover with affection is goodness. A heart that can embrace even the flowing waves is the foundation of goodness. However, due to the fall, all these hearts have collapsed.  
You must become a being who can respond with your body on the foundation of a heart that can overturn the entire universe. With a joyful heart, shout out to the world, and live a life that can nationalize and globalize what is undoubtedly good.  
The desire to go must be hundreds of times stronger than before to make one step forward in goodness. The problem lies with myself. Whose son will I become, and who will I take as my father? Everyone would want to be the son or daughter of the person who has the highest ideology of the time. If so, if we can call the one whom humanity most desires, the Creator of heaven and earth, our Father, there would be nothing more to wish for.  
A person who can be satisfied even in the lowest position is a happy person. Humanity cannot create even a single blade of grass by the roadside. We all want to become God's sons and daughters. The only way to become God's sons and daughters is to live righteously with the conviction that I will go even if the world opposes me. Then the world will yield.  
Throughout the long history, humanity has gone through the process to become God's sons and daughters, but all have failed in that process. Therefore, the faces of humanity bear the label of failure. When taking the test to become a son of God, how grateful would it be if someone could write the correct answers on my test paper when I know nothing? The one who can guide you through that process is the Messiah. While you write the answers yourself, the Messiah holds the pencil at the top. The Messiah is the one who teaches you the answers to be blessed as eternal sons and daughters of God with one hundred percent certainty.  
You have come here to become God's sons and daughters, right? Believe and obey. Then you will be saved at the final hurdle (the finals). The secret to becoming God's sons and daughters is to obey and follow the commands. God desires to make you His sons and daughters, and you also want to become God's sons and daughters, but inevitably, there will be the pains of childbirth involved. You must endure hardship. We are on the side of being created, so we must unconditionally yield to the side that is creating.  
After that, you will be able to say, "I am a son of God," or "I am a daughter of God." Then, as God's filial sons and daughters, you must take part in realizing God's ideal of creation.  
Jesus is the Son of God. However, to save all humanity, He carried the cross and walked the path to Golgotha.  
In the past, we could not serve the Father, but from now on, as the sons and daughters of the Father, we must live for the Father's will.  

Building the Kingdom and Living for Others  
<Summary of the message> God walked the path of suffering, starting from being a servant. How much have you struggled to escape from being a servant, and how much joy have you felt in breaking free?  
You must become the most loyal servant among servants and the most filial true children among children. How should you know this? You must know it in your heart. And you must feel it deeply in your bones.  
You must feel an explosion of gratitude when recalling the time you were in the position of a servant. Because you are called based on the ideology, even if the individual retreats, the ideology remains forever.  
What must we leave behind on our battlefield? It is heart. We must stand at the forefront. We must inherit the sorrow and sadness of heaven from the past 6,000 years.  
Heaven, which has fought like this, has come to this earth to establish true families before the will, aiming for the world of goodness. Therefore, we must fulfill the mission of serving the True Parents and provide them with rest.  
We must uphold the kingdom of goodness. We must bless the people of goodness and all things. This responsibility lies with us. When we fulfill this responsibility, God's sovereign world will be established.  
On August 1, 1963, at the former headquarters church.  
* This message is compiled from the notes recorded by former President Yoo Hyo-won. The title was added by the editor.  
Based on the establishment of Parents' Day and Children's Day, we can establish All Things Day. The Father, who had no nation and no people, will now restore the world starting from the individual. What we have proclaimed is truth along with heart.  
From now on, you must think that your houses, fields, and everything you own belong to the Father. You must recognize that they are public goods. Sin is the violation of public goods.  
We must establish families with public goods, build nations, and advance to the world. In this, the small must be absorbed.  
To treat without heart becomes a sin. We must treat material things with God's heart. Since heart is public, no one can govern it. We must value it through heart.  
The more you feel the sorrow of heaven at this time, the greater the blessing will be. God blesses you from the perspective of the entire universe, so you must establish this standard now.  
When you cannot fulfill your responsibilities, you must retreat. If you cannot fulfill your responsibilities, you must do so even in death.
We must become ancestors in the life of serving. All humanity in the world of death must stand in a position where they shed tears and serve. We cannot stand in a position where we become a burden and a source of worry.

No matter how difficult things may be, I have never blamed heaven. It is impossible to save the children of sin by lamenting from a miserable position. Even if we have to break apart blessed families, we must go forward.

When thinking of the will, you have forgotten the explosive indignation in your hearts. Family members living in Seoul must come to church every morning. The first of all things must be returned to heaven.

If heaven commands you to carry out the providence of restoration, can you do it? Now that you understand this will, you must live a life overflowing with emotion. Have you ever wept from Adam's position? Have you ever felt resentment from Noah's position? Is it not true that you have never experienced such things?

Among those who are indebted, you are among the indebted yet do not realize that you are indebted. You must become someone who knows the honor of gathering like this.

This place is not a church but your home. Disposing of church property at will becomes a violation of heaven and earth. Love the church. You must first pick up the broom and mop.

In times of tribulation, you must become the master of tribulation. If you have nothing to give, at least shed tears. Can such a person be rejected when a good era comes? No matter how wrong they (the government) may be, there is nothing to say. You only need to stand in a position where you can.

I have the historical material that can make the world weep with just one word. There is nothing to regret.

Three years is the period for finding children, and four years is the period for finding the land. The combined period is the seven-year great tribulation period.

The will of a father without a master
Genesis 1:27-31
<Prayer (I)> Heavenly Father, who is the Lord of all! We understand that all creation you have made must exist eternally with your ideals. We gather before your ideals, filled with joy and glory, and as the creation you have made offers praise as an object of joy, we have realized long ago that it is a great sorrow that we have not been able to live as your true sons and daughters, submerged in that glory, and we have regretted it for a long time.

The world of glory you have longed for, the Heavenly Father, should have been filled with joy, and that joy should have been the joy of all created beings, and that glory should have been the glory of all created beings, becoming one joy and glory. However, such an ideal standard has disappeared, and instead, we have been led into sorrow. All of this is due to human error, and we are well aware that it is the responsibility of us, the descendants of sinful humanity.

Every time we call upon you, we cannot help but feel the sorrow of the Father, and every time we look up to your image, we cannot help but feel anxious, as we are descendants who have betrayed heaven, holding the torch of sin, and it is infinitely regrettable and lamentable.

In order to hold onto such sinful us, God has left the hope of the heart of glory and has endured and longed for 6,000 long years. For the countless 6,000 years that you have labored because of us, because of our ancestors, because of the countless humans living on this earth today, and because of the countless spirits that remain in the realm of lamentation in the heavenly world, we are humbled before you and cannot help but confess once again that we are unworthy sinners.

Father, we are unworthy beings who cannot raise our heads before your great love, before your laborious hand, and before the footsteps of the wounded Father who has come to us. You have walked this path of tears. You have longed for humans to participate in this path, but humans have avoided it. Your heart wanted to share in such a miserable situation, but the humans who should be your children have often failed to understand that will and have driven nails into your heart.

Thus, we, who have been so unfilial, come before you again, kneeling and calling you Father. In your voice, there is infinite sorrow, and in your heart, there are grievances and choking circumstances. We understand that we must hold onto such a Father and call such a Father my Father and plead with you, and we also understand that you are a pitiful Father who must accept such circumstances.

However, as long as your will remains, and as long as you do not abandon that will, we must also hold onto you again while walking this path. We must seek forgiveness for having forgotten all of your sorrowful circumstances and for not having sought your forgiveness before you, Father, and we earnestly wish for your mercy.

The waves of death are today continuously polluting our living environment and occupying our surroundings, obscuring the glory of heaven. At such times, we must be mindful of what position we are in and what that position entails.

Today, we have been called before such a great providential will. We have been called without any merit. We have come to this place without any record of labor. We have come to this place without anything to offer before you. However, we have come with a heartfelt desire to confess our shortcomings with tears and to repent of our wickedness in order to hold onto you again.

We, who know the historical labor of the Father who had compassion on the circumstances of the prodigal son, have come seeking that connection with a heart of compassion, so please bind us again with your deep heart. Thus, we earnestly wish to be established as those who can go out into the world and fight.

This year is 1963, leaving behind a historic moment. At this time, we must awaken once again to the fact that we are to receive a new historical role and mission from the Father, and that we must bear the responsibility and mission from a position that cannot be replaced.

We must forgive all the historical labor of the past, along with the sins of this world, and while looking toward the new garden of hope, we must gather our hearts and bodies again, raise the flag of judgment, and as the soldiers of heaven, we must march forward in formation to confront the enemy world. The time is approaching when we must be mindful that this responsibility and mission are placed upon our shoulders, and we must strive to become true soldiers of heaven who can dedicate everything to the fight for an hour each day.

As we look at this world, this sinful world, we come to know that the end is near. At such times, we must fight with all our might in this final battle. We must become soldiers who can win in the final battlefield to resolve the grievances of heaven, so please allow this time to be one where we can once again make a solemn resolution and pledge before you, Father.

As we have been called before the providential will of the laborious Father, we repent once more for all the mistakes of the past that have caused concern, and we wish to become new sons and daughters who pledge to serve only you for the remainder of our lives. We earnestly wish to be those who are not lacking in appearing as the main characters of judgment in the new world.

This day is a holy day. It is a day when all people should praise the Father, and it is a day to serve the Father with all our sincerity. Therefore, wherever we call upon your holy name and praise you, Father, please bless us. Moreover, there are many of your sons and daughters scattered throughout this three-thousand-mile peninsula who are crying out with the heart of heaven and thinking of your heart, so please be with them as well. Also, please bless the countless sons and daughters of yours spread across the world. We earnestly wish that as time goes on, you will add to them the power of your love and your encouragement.

I earnestly wish and hope for this. May there be only glory in the will of the Father who plans victory. 

This evening, having heard the words, I earnestly ask that you allow us to make a new resolution and determination to fulfill the responsibilities of the owner before the providential will. I entrust everything to you, so please act according to your will. In the name of the Lord, I pray. Amen.

Now we have the materials and content to speak. Since we have entered the era of family restoration, we must save our relatives and families. You all know that this is the era of tribal restoration, right? Therefore, you must evangelize for families and for relatives. From August 1 to September 10, we have set a 40-day period, so during this time, you must evangelize with all your strength and with the determination to fulfill the faith you have followed the teacher with until now. 

A 4-Year Period to Establish the Foundation for the Restoration of All Things 

In the future, those who cannot evangelize must serve materially. This year, the teacher instructed the district leaders gathered from across the country to establish policies that can manage the regions because we must aim for qualitative improvement. 

So do not send just anyone for evangelism; select people who can uphold the dignity of the Unification Church. I believe they are currently doing that. 

The remaining people must dedicate themselves for 4 years, focusing on their districts, regions, or churches to establish the foundation for the restoration of all things. We must lay the groundwork for the restoration of all things by any means necessary. During these 4 years, we must establish an economic foundation that will not lose to any business organization in Korean society. 

Therefore, even if we cannot earn much, we must mobilize all we can earn each day. If you cannot evangelize, then engage in business or labor to fulfill the responsibility of the restoration of all things. You must not be irresponsible in establishing the standard for the restoration of all things. Whether poor or rich, everyone must fulfill their responsibilities according to their means.

When others wear fine clothes, we must be better than that. To do that, we must not lose to them.
